1. General Introduction
1.1 Assessment Objective
Provide the basis for decision making of relevant departments,
assure the projects reasonable and suitable in environmental aspect. and
make all the environmental problems be identified in the inception stage
of implementing the projects and be taken into consideration in the
process of site selection, planning and design. so as to make the
unfavorable impacts reduce to minimum level.
1.2 Basis for Compilation
1.2.1 Guohuan (86) File 003 Management of Project's
Environmental Protection
1.2.2 Huanjianjian 1993 File 324 Notification of Strengthening the
Environmental Impact Assessment Works of international
Financial OL ganization Aided Projects issued by NEPA,
National Plan Committee, Finance Ministry, Chinese People's
Bank
1.2.3 State EPA's Huanjianjian (1996) File 086 Returning Letter to
Opinions on ELT of Projects Aided bv World Bank loans in
Shandong
1.2.4 World Bank Expert's Preliminary Appraisal Memorandum

1.4 Assessment Principles and Methods
1.4.1 All the projects should be in accordance with the laws, regulations
and standards of environmental protection. The contents and depth of
assessment required by OD 4.01 of World Bank should also be obeyed on
the premise of executing the relevant regulations of EIA in China.
1.4.2 According to the sprits of the World Bank's Guidelines For ETA
(OD 4.01) and Notice on Strengthen EIA Jobs of International Monetary
Organization Financed Projects, all the projects with category A should
be proceeded overall assessment, comprehensively taken the favorable
and unfavorable impacts, long-term and short-term impacts, reversible
and irreversible impacts into consideration. To the project with categorv B,
onlv the main environmental problems are analyzed.
2. Summary of the World Bank Loaned Project
2.1 Survev
The World Bank loaned projects consist of six subprojects
distributed in three cities in Shandong province. There are two projects in
Jinan, one is the Jinan Yellow River Water Supply Pondage Reservoir
project, the other is Jinan Waste Water Network project. The other two
projects are Yantai 500 Heating Network project in Yantai city and
Weihai No.3 CHP Plant in Weihai citv. The Xiaoqing River Revolving
Funds Project and Yantai Demonstration Project of Cleaner Production
are not included in the scope of assessment.
2.2 Brief Introduction of World Bank Loaned Projects
2.2.1 Jinan Yellow River Water Supply Pondage Reservoir Project
The water is abstracted from Dawangmiao Sluice of Licheng District,
through the pump station to sedimentation basin, then transported by
deliverv pipeline to the reservoir. The reservoir is the water supplv source
of Jinan No.2 Water Purification Plant. The total and effective capacity of



the reservoir are 41.2 and 34.2 million m3, respectively. The inflow
volume is 8.65 to 9.65 m3/s with the average depth of 7.13 m. The length
of the box dam is 1 1.63 km.
2.2.2 Jinan Waste Water Networ k Project
This engineering is the conveyance svstem of Jinan Wastewater
Treatment Plant. The total area is 108 km2, which is the service scope of
the plant.
2.2.3 Yantai 500 Heating Netvork
The project is the construction engineering of heating network which
is used to transport the heat produced in Huangbohai CHP Company to
Zhifu District. The length of planned main pipeline network is 30.22 km.
There are 42 exchange stations. 2 pump stations and one boiler house of
peak load boiler.
2.2.4 Weihai No.3 CHP Plant Project
This plant is a newlv built plant with 3x75t/h high pressure fluidized
bed boilers and 2 sets of turbogenerator. The engineering includes the
CHP plant, steam pipeline network-, heat exchange station and hot-water
pipe network.
3. Natural and Social Conditions in Project Cities
3.1 Natural Conditions
3.1.1 Natural Conditions of Jinan
Jinan is located in 1160 12- l 7" 44 E, 360 02- 370 04'N with the
Mount Tai in its south and Yellow River in its north. It is hilly in its south
with the average height of 100-400 m above the sea level and in the
middle part with the average height of 40-100 m above the sea level, and
in its north is the alluvial plain with the average height of 2040 m above
the sea level. The basic landfonn in Jinan is higher in its south and north,
lower in its middle part witlh the shape of shallow plate.
3.1.2 Natural Conditions of Yantai
Yantai is located in 1200 -- 1230 E. 360 -- 380 N in the eastern part of
3



Shandong peninsula. In its east. south and north parts is the Yellow and
Bo Sea. In its west part is the Weifang and Qingtao Municipality. The
length from its east to west is 280 km, while in the direction from south to
north, the length is 130 km.
The project area is located in Zhifui District. It is adjacent to Muping
countv in its southeast. In its east and north, is the Yellow Sea.
The landform in Zhifu District is complicated with the typical
features of hilly region. The highest height in the district is 400 m above
the sea level. It belongs to eastern part of Jiaodong shield and northern
edge of Jiaodong raise region in geological structure.
3.1.3 Natural Conditions of Weihai
Weihai is located in 1210 -1230, 360 41- 370 35' N in the eastern
part of Shandong peninsula. Korea peninsula and Japan archipelago are
to its east and south across the sea. It is adjacent to Yantai in its west and
Liaodong peninsula to its north across the Yellow Sea.
Three directions around the Weihai urban area are hills and one
direction is the sea. The range of height is from 70 to 100 meter above the
sea level. In its seashore region is the plain whose soil structure is
composed of sand and alluvial laver caused bv marine deposit.
3.2 Social Conditions
3.2.1 Social Conditions of Shandong Pro-vince
Shandong province locates in eastern coastal area of China. Its area
is 156.700 km2 with the population of 86.71 million (population density:
553 per km2). It has 17 municipalities or its equivalencies, 139 counties
or county level cities or districts, and 46 cities. Shandong is one of the
provinces whose economic development is rapid. Its GDP in 1994 is
387.2 billion vuan ranked the third position in China. Its GDP will hit
640 billion yuan in 2000 according to the plan.
3.2.2 Social Conditions in Jinan
Jinan is one of historic cultural city and the birthland of Longshan
Culture. Jinan is a political, economic, cultural center of Shandong
province. It has five districts and counties. The urban area of Jinan is
2,119 km2 with the population of 5.3731 million. The density of
population in Jinan is 653 persons per km2.
4



3.2.3 Social Conditions in Yantai
Yantai municipality is a modem, international harbor city with high-
tech, commerce and trade, tourism as its main industries. It has
jurisdiction over 5 districts, 5 county level cities and 3 counties. The total
area of Yantai city is 13,500 km2 with the population of 6.3 million. The
project will be constructed in Zhifu District, which is the Yantai
municipality's political, economic, cultural center. The area of Zhifu
District is 47.4 km2 with the population of 0.4 million.
3.2.4 Social Conditions in Weihai
Weihai municipality is a provincial citY in Shandong. It has
jurisdiction over 1 district. 3 county level cities. The area of Weihai
municipality is 5436 km2 with population of 2.42 million. The people
living in urban area are engaged in industry and commerce . While in
rural area, the people are often engaged in agriculture, fishery and
aquaculture industry.
4. Predicted Impacts on Environment and Mitigation
Measures Taken
4.1 Jinan Yellow River Water Supply Pondage Reservoir
Project
4.1.1 Predicted Impacts on Enviroiunent
4. 1. 1.1 Impacts on Environment in Construction Phase
A. Impacts on Ecological Environment
The project will be constructed in the Northern Stretch Embankment
of Yellow River. The earth work will affect surrounding agri-ecological
environment.
B. Noise and Raise Dust
Transportation, vehicle and machines will bring about noise and
dust, which will affect the environment to certain extent.
C. Migration
5



There are 1186 persons of 300 households need resettlement. The
migration and land occupation will bring about certain impacts on living
and industrial activities.
4.1 .1.2 Impacts on Environment after Operation
The forecasting results of salinization and desertification of soil after
operation show that after adopting the seepage prevention measure,
digging penetration prevention ditches at the foot of reservoir's and
sedimentation basin's dam, the secondary salinization can be avoided.
After using of the sedimentation basins and sand stockvards, the
secondary ploughing is an effective method to prevent desertification.
The trend analysis of the reservoir's water quality show that'the
water qualitv in Yellow River is in a stable state. The first water just after
the Yellow River's drv-up is not suitable for abstraction.
After analogical investigation and assessment of Pucheng Reservoir
which has the same water source, geological and pollution sources
conditions as the Queshan's, we know that after five-vear's operation of
Pucheng Reservoir. its water is in middle eutrophic level, so we can draw
the conclusion that there is no danger of eutrophication for Queshan
Reservoir after its five-vear's operation. The control indexes for nitrogen
and phosphorus are 0.6 and 0.04 mglI, respectively.
4.1.2 Mitigation Measures
4.1.2.1 Seepage Prevention Measures of Reservoir
There is a soil film on the slope of box dam connected with another
soil film vertically buried under the ground of dam base to prevent the
seepage of the reservoir.
4.1.2.2 Around the box dam of the reservoir and sedimentation basin, the
seepage prevention and drainage measures will be taken to prevent the
soil's secondary salinization caused by the water level raise of
groundwater.
4.1.2.3 Redesign and re-planning of discharging system of farmland in
the project area.
4.1.2.4 Water Quality Assurance Measures
If the water level of the reservoir is lower than 24 meter. the water
6



will not be suitable for abstraction. Water delivery pipes will all be buried
under ground so as to reduce the impacts on surrounding environment
and protect the water quality.
4.1.2.5 Secondary ploughing measure will be taken to prevent the
sedimentation basins and sand stockvards from desertification after their
lifetime.
4.2 Jinan Waste Water Network
4.2.1 Predicted Impacts on Environment
4.2.1.1 Impacts on Environment in Construction Phase
Raise dust and noise in construction phase will have certain impacts
on environment and transportation. 1,460 persons of 310 households will
be resettled. 235.37 mu land will be occupied. The eighty three
enterprises and one school will be affected. The total cost for migration
and resettlement hits 64.7945 million yuan.
4.2.1.2 Impacts on Environment after Operation
After operation, the water quality in service area of project will be
improved and the pollution caused by wastewater's seepage will also be
mitigated. The operation of wastewater treatment plant will improve the
water quality of Xiaoqing River.
4.2.2 Mitigation Measures
Advanced machines. rational arrangement of construction time, high
construction efficiency, spraving water and covering of the soil will
reduce the impacts of noise and raise dust to minimum level.
4.3 Yantai 500 Heating Network Project
4.3.1 Predicted Impacts on Environment
4.3.1.1 Impacts on Environment in Construction Phase
*  Raise dust and noise produced in construction phase will have certain
impacts on surrounding environment.
* There will be certain impacts on transportation.
7



* The total area of land occupation is 43.125 m2. No resident houses
will be removed. Only 800 m2 house of village owned enterprise and
1,650 m2 building of Yantai Fuel Company will be demolished.
4.3.1.2 Impacts on Environment after Operation
A. Newly Added Air Pollution Sources
The newly added pollution source is the peak boiler. Its pollutants'
emission volume and concentration can accord with the national
standards. The maximum one-time concentration of S02 and TSP are
only 10.6% and 0.83% of corresponding standards, respectively.
B. Positive Effects
290 industrial boilers, 289 small boilers and domestic stoves will be
replaced after operation of the CHP plant. It will save 132,100 tons coal
for industrial use and 84,100 tons coal for domestic use annually. In
winter, the emission amount of S02 and TSP will reduce 6,808 and 4,403
tons, respectively. The removal rates of S02 and TSP are 20.2% and
34.14%.
The maximum removal rate of S02's and TSP's ground level
concentration will be up to 60% and 40%. The guarantee rate of 20% of
pollutants being removed is up to 60%.
C. Noise Impacts on Environment
Forty two pump stations are about to be constructed which will be
have certain impacts on some region at night, but the noise level does not
exceed the standard.
4.3.2 Mitigation Measures
4.3.2.1 Mitigation Measures in Construction Phase
* The pipeline network should be buried under the land which does not
have the natural resources.
* Strengthen traffic management, the main traffic lines and commercial
streets should not be selected as construction scope.
* Advanced low noise machines should be selected and the construction
should not affect the residents' rest.
* Spraying water on the sands and soils at the two sides of roads to
8



reduce the raise dust.
4.3.2.2 Mitigation Measures after Operation
A. Control Measure for Air Pollution
The water film dust removal facilities with the removal rate of 980/o
will be selected. The limestone will be added for desulfurization. (removal
rate: 50%). The dust is emitted through a chimney of 80 meter.
In coal yard, there is a water spraying instrument equipped.
B. Control Measure for Noise Pollution
Low noise machines and sound proof facilities are equipped.
C. Control Measure for Ash and Cinder
All the ashes and cinders are comprehensively utilized in brick
factory.
D. Control Measure for Water Pollution
Wastewater will be discharged into wastewater treatment plant.
4.4 Weihai No. 3 CHP Plant Project
4.4.1 Predicted Impacts on Environment
4.4.1.1 Impacts on Environment in Construction Phase
The impacts on environment in construction phase are from raise
dust and noise.
4.4.1.2 Impacts on Environment After Operation
A. Impacts on Atmosphere
* Impacts on Atmosphere of Newlv Added Pollution Sources
Under the stabilitv of B, C, D, the maximum landing concentration
of S02 and floating dust can meet the corresponding national standards.
In winter, the maximum dailv concentration of S02 is 0.0090 mg/m3,
9



accounting for 6% of the standard: the maximum daily concentration of
floating dust is 0.0021 mg m3, accounting for 1.4∞o of the standard; In
summer, the maximum daily concentration of S02 is 0.0080 mg/m3.
accounting for 5.33% of the standard: the maximum daily concentration
of floating dust is 0.0020 mg/m3, accounting for 1.33% of the standard
The axial concentration of S02 and floating dust under the adverse
meteorological conditions can meet the corresponding standards.
The annual daily average concentration of S02 is very low,
accounting for 3.33% of the standard.
* Positive Effects
The Weihai No. 3 CHP Plant will supply heat to all industrial
enterprises in the southern area of the city. It will replace 75 sets of
boilers and 15,000 small domestic stoves which bring a lot of wastes into
the air; therefore, the plant will help to improve ambient air quality in
Weihai after its operation. Cooperation among No. 1, No. 2 and No. 3
CHP Plants will begin soon and a network of heating is expected to be
built which helps to solve the problems of air pollution.
B. Impacts on Water Environment
There is small impacts on surface water environment due to the
wastewater of the CHP plant discharging to wastewater treatment plant.
There is no poisonous or harmful substances in the water discharged from
CHP plant. If the seepage prevention measures be taken, there is no
impacts on water quality of groundwater.
C. Impacts on Noise Environment
All the noise value of monitoring spots are lower than the standard.
There will be little impacts on environment if the noise control measures
are taken.
4.4.2 Mitigation Measures
4.4.2.1 In Construction Phase
A. Raise Dust Control Measure
A wall with the height of I to 2 meter will be built and water is
sprayed along the roads to prevent the raise dust from diff-using.
10



B. Noise Control Measure
Low noise equipment will be selected and construction at night is
forbidden.
4.4.2.2 Operation Phase
A. Control Measures for Air Pollution
Electrostatic facility with dust removal rate of 99.1 % will be adopted
and the desulfurization rate is up to 85% by using the fluidized bed boiler.
The chimney is 120 meter high.
B. Control Measures for Water Pollution
All the wvastewater are transported to wastewater treatment plant.
C. Control Measures for Ash and Cinder
Ash and cinder are transported to building material factory. There is
a revolving cinder vard in the plant and another vard for accident use in
the galley 1.5 km southwest to the plant.
D. Control Measures for Coal Dust
Timely spraying water will reduce the raise of coal dust.
5. Economic Benefits and Losses
After the implement of Shandong Environmental Protection Project,
the environmental quality in Jinan, Yantai and Weihai will be improved.
At the same time, the investment environment in these three cities will
also be optimized. It will push the development and open-up of the cities
forward, which brings about positive impacts on social and economic
development of Shandong province.
5.1 Jinan Yellow River Water Supply Pondage Reservoir
Project
After the operation of the reservoir, it can satisfy the need of water
supply in Jinan around year 2000, which will do good to groundwater
protection and recovery of Springs Landscape. The annual income of the
11



project wiIl hit 115.88 million yuan. The first-year's benefits w'ill be 7.767
million yuan. With the time going by, the income will have an ascending
trend.
5.2 Jinan Waste Water Network Project
After the completion of the network, there will be obviously' social,
economic and environmental benefits. All the wastewater in the service
area will be delivered to Xiaoqing River by the main pipes, including
220,000 m3/day wastewater discharged to the river after being treated in
the wastewater treatment plant. So the water pollution in the river
channels in urban area will be effectively collected and the pollution load
will thus be reduced. The daily removal amount of COD, BOD and SS are
88 tons, 53 tons and 81 tons respectively. After 11.29 year's operation, all
the investment can be paid back. The internal earning ratio is 22.34%/o.
The project's operation risk is small and 20 million yuan can be saved
annually after the treatment plant's operation. There also exists
immeasurable social benefits in perfecting city's overall function.
improving people's living standards, and promoting reform and open-up
in Jinan.
5.3 Yantai 500 Heating Network Project
The total investment of this project is 46.198 million US dollar. The
project's annual income is 19.83 million US dollar with a pay back period
of 8.6 years. The earning ratio of investment is 16.6% with economic net
value of 8.94 million US dollar. It will save 216.200 tons coal and
5.42x104 million Kwh electricity, 1.6x105 tons water annually. The
indirect economic benefits will hit 9.9814 million US dollar including
0.79 million US dollar compensated for land occupation. The saved land
area for constructing boiler houses will be 73,000 m2.
There are many low heat efficiency, low emission height small
boilers and domestic stoves which will be replaced by the project. It will
reduce 65,000 tons ash and cinder annually. The maximum removal rate
of S02's and TSP's ground level concentration will be up to 60% and
40%. The guarantee rate of 20% of pollutants being removed is up to
60%.
It will change the situation that pollutants' concentration exceeding
the standards every year, which brings about environmental benefits.
5.4 Weihai No.3 CHP Plant Project
12



All the economic indexes of the plant can meet the national
requirements. The pay back period of loans is 8.77 vears with the eaming
ratio of 20.03%.
After operation of the plant, 75 boilers and 15,000 domestic stoves
will be replaced. 4,116 tons of S02 and 2,189 tons of TSP will be
reduced. Construction of the plant will curb the deterioration of ambient
air quality in Weihai which has notable environmental benefits.
6. Environmental Adminiistration and Monitoring Program
6.1 Environmental Administration
The Shandong Provincial Environmental Protection Bureau and
local EPB are in charge of the environmental administration to
construction units. The administrative job will be in accordance with the
relative national regulations.
The construction units should have internal environmental
institutions, whose jobs are in charge of environmental administration and
monitoring, five to eight persons needed.
6.2 Monitoring Program
All the monitoring program of sub-projects will be implemented by
construction units and administrated by provincial and municipal EPB.
All the monitoring data should be reported to local EPB. The project
city's Environmental Monitoring Center will be in charge of the training
and monitoring quality examination.
6.2.1 Monitoring Program for Jinan Yellow River Water Supply
Pondage Reservoir Project
To ensure that the water quality can meet the Portable Water Quality
Standard, there are five spots set up in the proiect. The monitoring items
are as following: sand amount, PH, As, Hg, volatile phenol, total nitrogen.
total phosphorus, permanganate, total bacteria and coli-group. The
frequency of monitoring is once every month.
6.2.2 Mlonitoring Program for Yantai 500 Heating Network Project

The environmental measures must be implemented under the
administration of local EPB.

7. Public Participation
7.1 The Pattern of Public Participation
Based on the environmental and construction characteristics of each
sub-project, the investigation table was made to collect the suggestions
and attitudes of people who would be influenced by these projects.
Participants were mainly divided into several part as below: workers,
peasants, soldiers. merchants, students. teachers etc.
7.2 Investigation Result
120-500 investigation tables were distributed in each sub-project
and over 80% tables were returned. According to the investigation results,
83%.-95% participants thought it's necessarv for these projects to use the
World Bank loans. Most of them agreed that the atmospheric and water
environment would be improved in the area near the project, however,
they gave some suggestions to the projects, including the methods to
prevent and control the pollution should be considered bv the unit in
charge of construction during the process of building, especially the
influences of construction on the residents.
15



8. Assessment Conclusions
8.1 Jinan Yellow River Water Supply Pondage Reservoir
Project
The construction of the reservoir will increase 156 million m3 water
supply to Jinan annually. This will mitigate the tension situation in dry
years in Jinan, which will speed up the economic development in Jinan,
promote social stability, recover the springs landscape.
The project is composed of abstraction, sedimentation, water
delivery and storage parts. Either in construction phase or after operation,
there will be unfavorable impacts on surrounding environment. In
construction phase, land occupation, transportation, industrial and
artificial activities will bring about waste, raise dust and noise which have
certain impacts on surrounding environment besides the destroy of
vegetation. But, it will have little impacts on regional ecological
environment. The occupied land except the pits will be secondary
ploughing after two years. After the implement of the engineering, due to
the change of surface or groundwater's water level, it will cause the
water-logged and salinization of the soil, or desertification. After adopting
mitigation measures such as seepage prevention and discharging, step by
step using and second ploughing to prevent the desertification, the
unfavorable impacts will be reduced to minimum level. So this project is
feasible in environment. Moreover, all the mitigation measures are
feasible either in technology or in economy.
Three factors will affect the water quality in the reservoir after
operation. They are Yellow River's water quality, precipitation and dust.
If the water quality control planning, total discharge amount control and
feasible engineering measures are taken. the water pollution in the
reservoir will be avoided. The water quality in the reservoir will not
exceed the middle-eutrophic level.
8.2 Jinan Waste Water Network Project
After the implement of the project, the water qualitys in river
channels in the urban area will be remarkably improved. The pollutants
discharged into Xiaoqing River will thus be reduced.
On the premise of adopting practicable measures, a series of impacts
of the project on the social environment will be reduced. So the project
has notable social, economic and environmental benefits, which should be
implemented as soon as possible.
16



implemented as soon as possible.
8.3 Yantai 500 Heating Network Project
The project's impacts on environment are mainly in construction
phase. These kinds of impacts are temporary and reversible. If correct
measures are taken, the impacts will be reduced to minimum level. After
operation, the environmental benefits will be notable because it changes
the situation that pollutants exceeds the standards in sucessive years. Its
positive effects is greater than negative effects.
8.4 Weihai No. 3 CHP Plant Project
The construction of the project will curb the deterioration trend of
ambient air quality in Weihai. So, under the circumstance of correct
mitigation measures be taken, the project is feasible and necessary.
Generally speaking, if the Three Synchronization Principles is
persisted in and mitigation measures suggested in the reports are taken,
the projects' implement . will bring about great improvement in
environmental quality. So the Shandong Environmental Project is feasible
in environmental aspect.
17

Preface
The fast development of economy of Shandong Province lashes environment
greatly, envirorunental quality of some cities and rivers is tending to deteriorate
constantly. Shandong Province plans to apply for loan of World Bank to build(l 3 roup of
projects which can reduce the discharge of pollutants and improve enviroimental quality,
in order to prevent environment from deterioration and promote fine circle. After
discussion with World Bank, it is determined that Shandong Environmental Project is
composcd of six sub-projects and sofi projccts. Tne six sub-pro jces aie distribudted over
three cities( Jinan, Yantai and Weihai city ) of Shandong Province. Loan project of Jinan
area is composed of Jinan Queshan Pondcage RZeservoir for Yellow ltiver's Waler Suppiv

1.1 Purpose of Assessment and Guidelines
1.1. 1 Purpose of Assessment
Offering policv-making foundation for concerned departments. ensuring loan
projects are proper and reasonable to en-vironment. And ensuring any enviroiunenial
problem to be certain at the earlier stage of project so that it can be considered in
selecting address, planning and design of project and its adverse impact to environment
can be reduced to the lowest degree.
1.1.2 Guidelines
Wiith direction of concemed policies and environmental protection laws, making
Xfl1 use of present environmental impact assessment data and routine inspection data of
local environmental departments realized the purpose of developing economy and
protecting environment at the same time. Emphasizing charactenistic of project and
making area total amount control of polJutant.

measurement. Selecting assessment factor correctly. Analyzing environmenial impact of'

project in order to reduce it to lowest degree.

2.1 General Situation
On March, 27, 1993, Chinese Government and World Bank signed a 3-year
Rolling Loan Plan from 1993 to 1996. Shandong Urban Environmental Protection
Project Using World Bank} Loan is listed in Loan Plan of 97 Financial Ycar of World
Bank, and the loan quota is about 100 nillion dollars. Through repealed discussion with
World Bank, it is determined that Shandong Environmental Protection Project is mainly
composed of six sub-projects, Xiaoqing River Basin EnNironmental Protection Funds
and Yantai Clean-up Production Project of which are out of the assessment scope of
this Lirne. llie names, local cities and inivestinunt situation of othel fouI sub-project see

2.2 Brief Introduction of Sub-projects
2.2. 1 Jinan Yellow River's Water Supply (Q)teeshan Pondage
Reservoir Project
Abstracting water of Yellow Rtiver Irom Dawanigmiao sluice gale ol Lichleng
District by water-drawing pump stationi to scdimcntation arca, and thden tlhrough 1.3 knm
waterline, drawing water into planed reservoir which offers water for Jinan Yellow
River No.2 Factory by pump station.The storage capacity of planned Pondage reservoir
is 41200 thousand m3, efficient storage capacities 34200 thousand m3 and entering flow
of water of Yellow River is 8.65-9.65 m3/s. Perimeter of the reservoir is 11.63 km and
average storage deptlh is 7.13 m.
2.2.2 Jinan Urban Sewage Pipeline Network Prolject



The project is a conveyance system of Jinan Sewage Treatment Plant. Scope of
the project is the urban sewage main pipeline system in service limit of Jinan Sewage
Treatment Plant, the total area is 108 km2 and residential area of which is 61.6 kin2.
2.2.3 Yantai 500 Heating Network Project
The project is construction of heat-offering network and necessary facilities, which
offer Zhifu District of Yantai produced by Yantai Huangbuohai CIIP Plant in
simultaneous production of power and heat to realize mass heat supply. Planning to build
30.22 km first-class hot-water network, 42 heat-changing stations, 2 mtunk pumps and
one 4x29 MW steam dome.
2.2.4 Weihai No.3 CHP Plant Project
It is a new CBP plant, installed capacity of which is three 75t/h high-pressure
circular fluidized boilers and two CC12-4.9/0.98/0.294 steamers. The project includes
construction of CHP plant, steam network, first-class network and heating power station
etc.

3. Introduction of Natural and Social
Environment of Project City
3.1 Introduction of Natural Environment
3.1.1 Introduction of Natural Environrnent of Shandong Province
3.1.1.1 Geographic Environment
Shandong is coastal province of China. Geographical position:l 14'36'--122o43E,
34∞25'-38∞23'N. East-to-west length is over 700 kmn and south-to-north width is over
400 km. Land area of Shandong is 156.7 thousand km2, making up 1.6 percent of total
area of China.
Shandong Peninsula sticks out betveen Buo Hai and Huang Hai, western inland is
bounded by Hebci, Henan, Anhui and Jiangsu Province from north to south.
3.1.1.2 Climatic Environment
Clinmte of Shandong is classified in warm temperate monsoon climate. Eastem of
Peninsula has the characteristics of marine climate while Northwest Plain has
characteristics of continental climate. It is dry, windy and dusty in spring, hot and rainy
in summer, clear in autumn, cold and short of rain and snow in winter. The annual
average temperature is 11-140C, increasing progressively from peninsula to inland. The
annual average precipitation is 500-1000 mm.
3.1.1.3 Fresh Water Environment
Shandong is situated in middle latitude zone with little precipitation. so the area of
surface fresh water is small. The area of surface fresh water of whole province is about 4
million mu, not as much as 2 percent of land area. There 5000 rivers longer thlani 5 ki;
and 18 rivers longer than 100 km, but most of them are seasonal rivers which are steel)
and fast. The water lost is much more than that permcating underground, and water
existing on the surface is more little. The major lakes are Southern Four Lakcs and
Dongping Lake. There are 5000 big or small reservoirs within the boundary of province.
Yellow River is a river passing through Shandong Province. It enters at
Shishuanglou of Dongmning County of Southwestem Shandong, runs towards northeast
through 6 cities and 21 counties of Northwest Plain and pours into Buo Hai at Kenli
County. The river in Shandong Province is 571 km long.
3.1.1.4 Sea Environment
Shandong is a coastal province. XVide seas and plentiful sea resource are
advantageous to economic development. Only the area of shallow seas 170 thousand
km2, which is 1.1 time of land area of Shandong. The land coastline is 3121 km and
3-1



island coastline is 683 km. which add up to 3805 km.
3.1.2 Introduction of Natural Environment of Jinan
3.1.2.1 Geographical Environment
Jinan is situated in 1 16012'-1 17044∂ and 36002'-3704'N, at the south of Yellow
River and the north of Mount Tai on the north of Middlesouthern Mountainous Region
and contiguous to Yellow River Alluvium Plain towards north. Terrain is long and
narrow from east to west, and high in south and low in north. The south of Jinan is
mountainous and hilly land with an average elevation of 100-400 mn; the middle is plain
with an average elevation of 40-100 m; the north is alluvial plain with an average
elevation of 20-40 m; at the north end is the ground river--Yellow River with a 30 m tall
dam, which fonn the shallow-dish basic terrain which is lower in middlc and high in
south and north.
3.1.2.2 Climatic Characteristics
Jinan is classified in warm half-humnid continental monsoon climate, the four
seasons of which are distinctive. It is dry and windy in spring, hot and rainy in sumuner,
clear and pleasant in autumn and cold and dry in winter. The average temperature is 14.2
0C, annual average precipitation is 685 mm, annual average wind speed is 3.2mts. The
perennial dominant wind in southwest, wind frequency is 39.4%; the sub-dominant wind
is northeast wind, wind frequency is 30.4%.
3.1.2.3 Rivers
There are two river systems such as Yellow River and Xiaoqing River. Yellow
River enters at Changqing County, through Licheng and Zhangqiu, then runs along the
northern boundary towards Zouping. The river within boundary is 134 km long.
Xiaoqing River rises spring of Jinan, runs through Licheng, Zhangqiu and Zouping, and
pours into sea at Yangjiaogou of Shouguang County. The whole river is about 240 km
long while it in Jinan is 76 kn long.
3.1.2.4 Hydrology and Geology
The hydrogeological condition of Jinan is complex. Cambrian and Ordoiician
carbonate rock stratum is distributed in south hill region. Rain water permeates
underground and becomes crevice karst water. It flows towards north, gushes out and
becomes spring group when it is obstructed by gabbro.
3.1.3 Introduction of Natural Environment of Yantai
3.1.3.1 Geographical Environment
3-2



Yaitai is situated on the east of Shandong Peninsula , geological position: 120'-
123∞E and 36∞-38∞N. It is closed to Huang Hai and Buo Hai at the east, south and north
and contiguous to Weifang and Qingdao city at the west. It is 280 kn long from east to
west and 130 km wide from north to south.
Project site-Zhifu District of Yantai is on the north of Shandong Peninsula,
geological position: 112∞24'E and 37∞24'N. It is closed to Huang Hai at the north and
east and stands facing Dalian at the north. It is contiguous to Muping at the southeast and
bordered to Fushan District at the west and southwest with the boundary of Jia River.
Terrain of Zhifu District is complex, it is a typical hilly region with an average elevation
of 400m. Urban district is on the northern edge of Jiaodong lump region.
3.1.3.2 Climatic Characteristics
Zhifu District is classified in warm temperate monsoon climate. The change of
season and monsoon is distinctive while the daily temperature change is small. It has
Characteristics of plentiful precipitation, moderate rainfall and clement climate. The
annual average temperature is 12.4∞C, annual average precipitation is 749 mm and
annual average wind speed is 4.2mls. Annual dominate wind is southwesten winid.
3.1.3.3 Rivers
The seven mnain rivers are Dagujia River, Qu River, Heng River, Le River, Majiadu
River, Guangdang River and Xingfu River etc.. The length of all rivers within boundary
is 71.7 km while the boundary length of Dagujia River is 22.8 km.
3.1.4 Introduction of Natural Environment of Weihai City
3.1.4.1 Geographical Environment
Wcihai is situated on the cast end of Shandong PenirLsular, Gcographical position:
121011'E and 36041'-37035N. It is surrounded by sea on three sides. It stand.s facing
Korea Peninsula on the east and facing Japanese islands on the south across sea. It is
separated from Liaodong Peninsula by Buo Hai Strait on the north and contiguous to
Yantai on the west.
The urban distnict of Wcihai is surrounded by mountains on three sides closcd to
sea on one side. It is classified into hilly region with an average elevation of 70-100 m.
The coast land is smooth and layer structure is sedimentary fine sand layer and impulsive
layer.
3.1.4.2 Climatic Characteristics
Weihai city is classified in middle latitude monsoon climate. It is marinle climate
wiffi characteristics of cold spring, cool summer, warm autumn, lukewarm winter,
plentiful wind and great humidity. Its temperature varies slightly in day and at night and
3-3



its verdant perod is long. The annual average precipitation is 760.7 mm. The annual
average temperature is 12. 1∞C. Dominant wind is northwestem wind.
3.1.4.3 Rivers
The main rivers are Wuzhe River, Yangting River, Xujia River and Zhangcun River
etc. They are classified in nai river, source of which is near but length of which is short.
The basin area and flow is small while the seasonal change is large.
Geographical position of project cities see Chart 3.1.
3.2 Introduction of Social Environment
3.2.1 Introduction of Social Environment of Shandong Province
Shandong is situated on the east coast of China. Its total area is 156.7 thousand km2
and its total population is 86710 thousand. Its density of population is 553/kn2. It is
composed of 17 cities(prefectures), 139 counties and 46 cities. Shandong is one of the
provinces the economy of which develops fast. Its GDP in 1994 is 387.2 billion yuan,
ranking third all over the country, and is planned to amount to 640 billion yuan in 2000.
3.2.2 Introduction of Social Environment of Jinan
Jinan is one of the famous cities of historn and culture. It is the birthplace of
Neolithic Longshan Culture. Now Jinan is the capital of Shandong Province, is the
political, economic and cultural center of whole province. It is composed of 5 districts
such as Lixia, Shizhong, Tianqiao, Huaiyin and Licheng District and 5 counties such as
Zhangqiu, Changqing, Pingyin, Shanghe and Jivang, urban area is 2119 km2. Total
population amounts to 5373.1 thousand and density of population is 653/km2. Jinan is
comprehensively developing city with industry as its main body. It has formed an urban
industrial system with 35 industrial departmcnts with machine. metallurgy, chemistry, oiL
building materials, light industry, textile and paper-making as its main bodv.
3.3.3 Introduction of Social Environment of Yantai
Yantai is a modernized and international port city vith advanced technological
industry, trade and tour as its main bodv. It is composed of five districts, five cities and
three counties, its total area is 13.5 thousand km2 and population amounts to 6.3 million.
The project area-Zhifu District is the political, econornic and cultural center ol Yantai.
Its total area is 47.4 km2 and its population amounts to 400 thousand.
3.3.4 Introduction of Social Einviroilnient of Weihai
Weihai was promoted to prefecture citv in 1987 by sanction of the State Council. It

4 Environmental Impact and Mitigation
Measures in Jinan Project Area
4.1 Environmental Impact and Mitigation Measures of Jinan
Yellow River Water Supply Pondage Reservoir Project
4.1.1 Project Analysis
4.1.1.1 Location
The project area is located in the end of north stretch zone, northern bank of
Yellow River, facing urban area of Jinan across the river, belonging to Daqiao Town of
Licheng District. Jinan is located in 36 02' to 37 31' N and 1160 11' to 1170 44' E,
which is in middle west part of Shandong Province. The topography of Jinan is higher in
its south and lower in its north. Southem area of Jinan is hilly and, middle and northem
parts are plains. The elevation of urban is 30 to 40 meters above the sea level.
0 Location of abstraction site: The Queshan Reservoir's abstraction site is located in
north of Jinan, northem bank of Yellow River. The Luokou hydrometric station is
located in 2.5 kilometers upper reaches of the abstraction site, using Dawangniao
abstraction gate, which was established in 1995, between the twelfth to sixteenth
darns of Dawangrniao's dangerous section.
*  Location of sedimentation basin: The sedimentation basin was selected at the back
of dangerous section of Dawangmniao to 309 highway. The length and the width are
about 3.2 kilometers and from 0.3 to 0.7 kilometer.
*  Location of Queshan Reservoir: Queshan reservoir is located at the end of north
stretch zone of Yellow River, facing the Yellow River's dam in the east and north
stretch zone in the north. It is adjacent to the former railway from Beijing to
Shanghai in the south. The axis area of the dam is 6.08 square kilometers. The 308
and 309 highway are 1,700 meters to the north and 1,000 meters to the southwest of
the reservoir, respectively. See location chart.
4.1.1.2 Brief Introduction to the Proiect
4.1.1.2.1 Chier Function and Property or the Project
The chief function of the project is to guarantee the water supply from Yellow
River during the river's dry-up period so as to solve the city's water shortage problem, to
meet the city's need for water for its economic development and its residents' daily life
and to restore Jinan's spring scenery. The property of the project is newly built.

4.1.1.3 Water Supply Target of the Project
Water supply target of the project is to guarantee a daily supply amount of 367
thousand tons during a Yellow River dry up period of 81 consecutive days.
4.1.1.4 Scale of Water Diversion and Water Supply of the Project
4.1.1.4.1 Scale of Water Supply from the Reservoir to WVater Plant
According to the design of the project, an amount of 440 thousand tons is to be
supplied to Shawangzhuang Yellow River No. 2 Water Plant and an amount of 367
thousand tons dunng the river's dry-up period. If the water loss in pipeline be 1%, then
the daily water from the reservoir will be 444 thousand tons and 370 thousand tons
during the river's dry-up period. The designed volume of flow is 5.14 m3/s and 4.28
m3/s.
4.1.1.4.2 Scale of Water Inflow into the Reservoir
Based on thc number of days when water is available in Yellow RZiver ( 97%o
guaranteed ) and the reservoir's water supply plan, plus evaporation and leakage, the
pump station's volume of inflow is 8.65 m3/s and increases to 9.38 m3/s during Julv
through September every year.
4.1.1.4.3 Scale of Aqueduct's Water Diversion
Based on the inflow scale, evaporation in the sedimentation basin, water loss of 5%
leak-age and a water loss of 3% in sand convey the designed water diversion scale of the
aqueducts is 9.34 m3/s and increases to 10.14 during July through September every year.
4.1.1.5 Overall Layout of the Project
4.1.1.5.1 Industrial Process of the Reservoir
Water is to be firstly diverted from Yellow River through Dawangmiao diversion
sluice and then pumped into the sedimentation basin. Preliminary sedimentation basins
are all along the river embankment. Through 1.3 kilometer's pipeline, the water is to be
sent from the sedimentation basins to an intake pump station which in tum pumps the
water into the pondage reservoir. then the water will be sent to Shanwangzhuang Water
Plant through an outflow pipeline which spans the Yellow River for about one kilometer.
The mud will be dredged and pumped to sand stock-yard through mud pumps. See
Figure 4.1.1 and Figure 4.1.2.

except some changes in the anTangement outside the Northem Stretch Embankment. The

scenarios are the same.
4.1.1.6 Main Contents of the Project
4.1.1.6.1 Canal Pump Station Diversion Project and Chief Indexes
The canal pump station locates behind Dawangmiao Divesion Sluice and is a level
I pump station. It's designed volume of flow is 10.6 m3/s and the designed anti-flood
water level is 30.8 meters. It has 6 sets of pumps with a total capacity of 6x280 kW. Two
of which are in reserve.
4.1.1.6.2 Sedimentation Project and Chief Indexes
The project will use sedimentation ditches which is more than 700 meter at is
utmost width, 3.3 kilometers long, 24.2 to 24.5 meters high. The utmost alluvial height
of the ditch is 32.3 meter and the highest water position is 32.5 meters. Designed term of
use is 25 years. The area from Dawangmiao to Yueva dam usable for sedimentation is
1.4 square kilometers. The sedimentation ditch is going to be used stage by stage. The
first stage is the continuous depositing stage. The bankl will be built up to 29 meters
4-3



during the first phase of construction. the using water level being 27.5 meter. It thfe
expected continuous using term is three vears, during which time aggregate diversion
volume of water will be 524,724,600 cubic meter, diversion volume of sand, 3,573,500
cubic meter, sedimentation volume of sand, 3,241,700 cubic meter, sand volume into
the reservoir, 331,800 cubic meter, sedimentation rate, 0.91.
The second stage is the applied stage during which the height of the bank will be
increased by one meter yearly and the applied water level will be increased by one meter
annually, ensuring no less than two meter's depth of the applied water. The utmost
height of the bank will be 32 meters. In this stage, the term of usage will be three years,
during which time the volume of diversion and sedimentation will be the same as in the
first stage, aggregate deposit of sand will be 3,266,200 cubic meter and 307,300 cubic
meter of sand will be discharged into the reservoir and sedimentation rate Will be 0.91.
In the third stage, two ditches will be used instead of the usage of one ditch. The
highest applied water level will be 32.5 meters, the height of the bank will be 33.5 meters.
The sand will be disposed by means of " dealing with sedimentation vith digging",
transported to the sand stockyard through the sand transporting pipe witl the assistance
of the dredge. The method will last until the 25th year, the annual volume of water
diversion being 174,908,200 cubic meter, volume of sand diversion, 1,191,200 cubic
meter, sand deposit, 1,012,400 cubic meter, volume of sand discharge into the reservoir,
178,800 cubic meter, sedimentation rate, 0.85.
The term of usage of each stage and the sand content of ciitches will be shown in
Table 4.1.1.

4.1.1.6.7 Flood Discharge Sluice Project
The purpose of this sluice is to prevent or miniiize the loss of accidents and to
lower the water level or empty the reservoir. The project uses Dawu water discharge
sluice which will be rebuilt for flood discharge. Its designed water level will be 29.87 m,
dead water level 24.0 m, sluice plate bottom 21.5 m high. Water discharge rate will be 40
m3/s. The process of discharge is shown in Table 4.1.5.
Table 4.1.5     Discharge process of the reservoir

As shown in the chart, it will take 10.31 days to discharge water from the highest
water level of the dead water leveL that is 24 rn, water discharged 34.2 million m3. It will
take 12.35 days to empty the reservoir, discharging 41.2 million m3.
4.1.1.6.8 Irrigation and Discharge Project
A. General Introduction to Original Irrigation and Discharge Project
Originally the end of the north stretch area was part of the area irrigated by water
leaking from the Yellow River. At the head of the ditch, behind the inflow sluice, there
are 3 main ditches which lie in the east, west and north, and sedimentation area, pondage
reservoir and other accompanying constructions. The discharge project consists mainly
of Qiji River and Dash River- the two main discharge ditches and branch ditches, and
the discharge sluice project, etc.
4-7



At present, 3 mnain ditches and 2 discharge ditches and part of the branch ditches
and the accompanying constructions have been completed. Thie cast main ditch fi-om
Nanfang Village to Queshan, is 6 km long, with the designed flow volume of 3 m3/s.
The west main ditch, from the sluice to Dingkou Village of Sangzi Town, is 6.4 km long
with the designed flow volume of 2 m3/s. The north main ditch, from the sluice to Sundi
Town in Jiyang by way of Highway 308 and Dawvu sluice, is 15 km long with the
distance of 2.8 km from Dawangmiao to Dawu. The original 25 km's main discharge
ditch, at the end of the north stretch area, joining Dashi River from Nanfang Village via
Dawu discharge sluice, is now added with main ditches and tunnel sluice project.
B. Outline of the rIigation Project of the Area after the Completion of the Project
The reservoir project, after completion, will have great effect on the original
discharge system. The 4 km long main discharge ditch from Nanfang Village to the north
stretch embankment and Dawu discharge sluice will be used by the reservoir. In order to
ensure the passage of discharging, it is planned to dig a discharge ditch along the
northern side of the pondage reservoir and the former I Iighway 309, from Dawu flood
discharge sluice to the outside of the northem stretch embankment, thcn from the
embankment to Dasiti River. The ditch will be 6.95 km long, 3.85 km of whichl along the
northern stretch cmbankrment will be used togethlc witlh leakage prevenition ditch.
Furthermore, the change of the discharge system entails the constrnction of 10 new
bridges.
4. 1. 1.6.9 Power Supply Project
From Dawangmniao No.1 pump station to the pondage reservoir, and then to
Yellow River No.2 Water Plant, the whole water source project has 3 pump stations with
a total power capacity of 3145 kw. The sedimentation basin No.1 pump station requires
1680 k-w, the inflow pump station (No.2) requires 465 kw, and the outflow pump station
(No.3) requires 1000 kw. The 3 pump stations are all accoutered with transforners.
4.1.1.6.10 Transportation Project
When the project is completed, the pondage reservoir will cut off Jinan-Dezhou
Highway 104. It is planned to built a motorway, about 2.5 km long, from Jidan Highway
309 at the point 500 m from Wangiiazhen northNvard to Highway 308. Besides, to
guarantee the management and function, a 7m wide asphalt road will be built on the top
of the embankment of the reservoir.
4.1.1.6.11 The Grade of the Project
The project of Dawangmiao sluice, which takes water from the Yellow River, is of
grade I. In the sedimentation channel project, bunding tunnel is of grade II, and others
are grade m.
Queshan Reservoir has a designed capacity of 41.2 million m3 and is a niiddle-sized
plain reservoir of grade m. The main construction is designed according to grade II's
4-?



standards. The northem embankment is a flood prevention project of grade I. The
embankment, except the Dawu discharge sluice modificatio  pi-ojcct (gradc l), is of
grade II.
The outflow pipeline project is of grade fl. The pipelines across the Yellow River
are of grade I and the rest is of grade III. Construction of the discharge sluice is of grade
L
4.1.1.6.12 Total Investment and Chief Indexes of the Project
The project will cover 12819 mu of land and dig 2.0241 million m3 of earh. Earth
replaced is 6.1351 million m3. Total amount of concrete is 80.382 thousand m3. It also
need 1.4909 million ordinary workdays. Chief matexials consumption: 5370 tons of steet
2063 m3 of timber, 34913 tons of cement and 7569 tons of diesel oil.
Static investment of the project is 469 million yuan. TIotal investment amounts to
499.4598 million yuan.
4.1.2 Investigation and Assessment of Environmcntal Quality
4.1.2.1 Investigation and Assessment of Existing Situationi of'
Pollution Sources
From the result of investigation of poliution sources, there are no large or middle
size enterprises. There are only 50 small size enterprises in the project area which have
no poUlution or light pollution. The industrial zone of Daqiao town lies in about more
than 2 kilometers away from the reservoir. The enterprises within the industrial zone are
of none pollution or light pollution which will not be harm to the reservoir.
Briquette is the main fuel consumed in the area for cooking and heating. The
annual coal consumption amount of residents is from 5,480 to 6,850 tons. The annual
discharge amount of S02, NOx and TSP are from 175.4 to 219.2 tons, 19.8 to 24.8
tons, 274 to 342 tons, respectively.
4.1.2.2 Monitoring and Assessment of Environmental Quality
The environmental quality assessment will be proceeded on the basis of
monitoring of Yellow River's water, substrate sludge, groundwater and soil.
The monitoring sections are shown in Fig. 4.1.3. The assessment standard of
Yellow Rivers water is Class 3 standard of National Surface Water Quality Standard
(GB3838-88); class 3 standard of Groundwater Quality Standard (GB/T14848-93) will
be adopted for groundwater, background value of moisture soil will be adopted for
substrate sludge and soil. Single-factor-index method is adopted for assessment. the
assessment results are shown in Table 4.1.6 to Table 4.1.9, respectively.

The results of monitoring and assessment of water qualitv in Yellow River show that
in the inception stage of the river having current, there are relatively severe pollution of
ammonia nitrogen, total notrogen and total mercury. The concentration of ammonia
nitrogen in spot 1 and 2 are 1.80 and 1.99 mg/I, which are 8 and 8.85 times more than
the corresponding standards, respectively. The concentration of total nitrogen in spot 1
and 2 are 4.88 and 5.09 mg/I, which are 3.88 and 4.09 times more than  lhe
corresponding standards, respectivelv. The concentration of total mercun in spot 1 and
2 are 0.00032 and 0.00021 mg/l, which are 2.2 and 1.1 times more than the
corresponding standards, respectively. Other factors of water quality are up to the
corresponding standards. The first reason that anmmoniia nitrooen, total nitrogen, total
mercury exceeding the respective standards is in 1996, there were 132 days drl-up in

4.1.3 Analysis of Factors Influencing the Environnment
Analysis of the project's environment-influencing factors is carried out in three
ways. One is the projects impact on the environment during its construction period.
The other is the reservoir's impact on the enwironment when it is put in use. Ihe
third one is the environment's impact on the prqoect.
4.1.3.1 The Impact of Duration under Construction on
Ecological Environment
According to the construction plan, the duration under construction will last
about two years. The impact of duration under construction on ecological
4-13



environment will depend on job practice, construction season, features of
engineering, topography, landforms and ecological status to a great extent.
4.1.3.1..1 The Impact on Vegetation
In addition to reduction of vegetation rate caused by the land occupation of
sedimentation basin, water delivery engineering and reservoir, the tentative
occupation of lands such as tentative houses, roads, parking area, treading of people,
roller compaction of machineTy will also bring about damages to vegetation. The
engineceing activities like carthwork and filling of dam foundation will make carth's
surface naked, this will bring about soil losses to a certain extent if theie is a big rain.
The impact will be mainhl imposed on the crops in the farmland because of the
plain landform in the project area. This kind of impact will be recovered atler one
to two years except that of caused by earthwork. It will not have an) great impact
on ecological environment.
4.1.3.1.2 Impacts of Noise and Raise Dust on Environment
In the peak-hour of construction, the construction of sedimentation basin,
water delivery pipeline and reservoir will be conducted simultaneously. According
to monitoring data of other large scale reservoir, the noise will be up to 70 to 90 dB
around the scope of 200 meters of working face. Moreover, the tail gas of motor
vehicle and flying ashes will do harn to the surrounding environment. But it will do
little harm to the villages due to the long distance.
4.1.3.1.3 The Impact of Wastewater and Solid Waste
The domestic wastewater and solid waste being produced within the
construction period will bring about negative impact on ecological environment if
these are discharged without due treatment. The destroyed crops and lands during
the construction should be compensated. This kind of impact will be eliminated
after completion.
4.1.3.1.4 The Impact on Transportation
During duration under construction, part of the road from Jinan to Dezhou
will be occupied, the measure which is about to taken is to build a tentative road.
4.1.3.1.5 Migration and Settlement
The acreage occupied b) the engineering includes twvo parts. One is 7.19
square kilometer used for constructing reservoir. The other is about 1.11 square
kilometer, which is occupied by sedimentation basin.
The total household of migants is 304 with the population of 1,186
4-14



(including: male, 733; female, 453).
The migration will have impact on the migrants to a certain exient. So, a action
plan for migration and resettlement had been drafled. The budget for land
occupation and migration are 50.49 and 69.48 million yuan, respectively, with a
total of 119.97 million yuan to reduce the unfavorable impact of the project.
4.1.3.2 Analysis and Forecast of Project's Impact on Environment
after Construction
4.1.3.2.1 Analysis and Forecast of Project's Impact on Geology
The main impact on geology is from construction of the reservoir and
sedimentation basin.
A. Geological Features in the Construction Area
The project area locates on the Jinan rock mass of Luxi breakl and bulge region
with the Qihe-Guangrao break on its north, Qianfoshan break on its east, Ganggou
break on its west. This area belongs to monocline structure. From the Quaternary
period, this area belongs to slight uplifted region. The flood drainage area. on the
north of the Yellow River, locates in the low-lying zone formed by northward
movement of the crust. See Fig 4.1.4 and 4.1.5.
The project site lies on the alluvial plain of the Yellow River. The top la! er of
the river course is the new alluvial deposits which is chiefly yellow sand soil (alQ4)
with some fine sands or clay lens. Its thickness can be 20 m at its utmost. The
bottom layer is AIQ3 which is gray and brown soil and clay with calcium blocks in
hard plastic form. Within the exploration depth (20 m) on either bank are mainly
the yellow sand soiL soil and clay, mostly in plastic or soft plastic forms. The rocks
under the north bank are complcx. The old desolate river course shallowly covered
under the reservoir area is mainly made up of fine sands.
Jinan rock mass (V3/5) is under the Quatemary stratum and crops up only at
Mount Queshan north of the river, Yaoshan, Jinniushan, Biaoshan, Manshan,
Sushan on the south. The so-caIled " Nine Points in Shandonig's Fog" refers to the
nine mountains. The area of Jinan rock mass is about 464 km2 whose lilhology is
complex basite. The rocks are chiefly gabbro, diorite and sinaite, etc. Its main body
stretches from east to west, 45 km long and 20 km wvide. Most of the rock mass is
covered bv the Quatemary stratum. The rock mass has an out-stretching contact
with the surrounding rocks with an angle of 60 and the rock mass is like a cover on
the top. There is also some granite in the rock mass. So the project has a good
stability on this solid rock mass.
The northern part of the rock mass is 02 Ordoxician limestonie. In fiirtler
north it is C+P carbon sestem plus Dyas seratum till the south of the Qihe-
Guangrao Break. And the 3rd stratum appears under the Quatemary stratum.

B. Geological Conditions of Reservoir and Sedimentation Basin
The earth within the exploration depth of Queshan Pondage Reservoir's
bundings can be categorized into 3 layers. The first layer is mainly artificial sand
soil fillings, about 23.0-33.06 m in altitude, 8-9.6 m in thickness with some soil and
clay in. The second is the alluvial layer covering the reservoir site, about 3-6 m in
thickness, part of which is the old desolate river course, such as the distance from
Pale No.5+700 to No.6+100 which is 15 m deep with mainly sand soil plus some
clay, soil, fine sand layer or lens. The third laver is the river and lake sedimentation
layer (al+1Q4), generaly at 18-20m beneath with mairdy soil and layers of clay,
sand soil or lens occurring altemately. The fine sand layer between Pale No.7+000
and 8+000, 9+200 and 9+800 constituted the old river course.
Although the perviousness of the soil and clay in the 3rd layer is smaller than
0.01 m/d and can be viewed as a water-proof layer, it is not continuous, and thick
enough. The sand soil layer surrounding the reservoir, especially the fine sand layer
in the old liver course is the main Icaking area. Undcr the action of a @ig} water
head, land slide might occur, flooding the reservoir, causing salinization and
swamping. Saturated sand soil and fine sand layer are all easily liquified, thus
measures must be taken to avoid leakage and to discharge water.
The ground water level ini the reservoir is generally 21.5 m. The earth of the
sedirnentation's bundings can be categorized into 3 layers and 2 inter-layers from
top to bottom. The first layer is sand soil, 0-4 m thick, plastic-softplastic in form.
The second layer is soil which is plastic, 10 m thick and is the nmain part of the
sedimentation basin. In this layer are many thin layers or lens which can be
categorized into 3 interlayers according to their lithologv. The first interlayer is
alluvial mud or alluvial earth with a stench smell in the soft-plastic or fluid-plastic
form and in the shape of lens. Its maximum thickness is 2.4 m. The second
interlayer is plastic orange clay with a thickness of 0.8-2 rn, ZK4+337 can be more
than 4.0 m. The third interlayer is plastic sand soil; ZKO+868-1+710 and
ZK2+340-3+194 are continuous and the thickness is less than 4.0 m. The land in
the sedimentation basin is low-lying. The ground water is 1.0-1.5 ni beneatll;
elevation 23.00 m.
C. Hydrogeological Conditions
The ground water in this area is mainly the ventage water of the Quaternary
stratum. The chief water-containing layers are the sand soil layer and fine sand Layer.
Compensation for the ground water comes from the atmnospheric rainfall and
Yellow River's side leakage. The depth of ground water varies with the season and
the distance to the river. Normally it is 1.0-2.5 m beneath the earth and the water
quality is good and there is no erosive C02. Ventage pressure-bearing water is
normally 20 m beneath and is of fine quality and abundant in amount. Its water
levcl is 0.5 m lower than the hydrobath.
4-1 6



D. Analysis of Project's Impact on Environmental Geology
From the above-mentioned geological conditions of the project site, the
reservoir and the sedimentation basin, we can see that the rock break in the area is
not well developed. Besidcs, the scale of the reservoir is not very big, leakage
amount is small and the leaking water will compensate for the Quatemary stratum's
ventage water. Therefore there won't be any direct influence on the rock break.
And, on historical records between 1970 and 1995, there were 19 earthquakes of
1.0-3.3 level in this area, which thus belongs to the earthquake inactive area.
According to China's Earthquake Severity Illustration Map (1980 Edition), the
project locates in a VI level area. The pondage reservoir and sedimentation basin
won't bring about any earthquake.
The reservoir, sedimentation basin and sand stockyard arc low-lying. The
surrounding sand soil layers, especially the fine sand layer in the old river course are
the chief leakage area. Under the action of a high water head, flooding and
secondary salinization may occur.
4. 1.3.2.2 Forecast of the Project's Impact on Soil's Secondary
Salinization
A. Groundwater's Impact on the Soil's Salt Content
The salt in the ground water is the source of soil salt. Ground water level
influences the soil's salt content. Researches in Dezhou Ling County by Agriculture
Research Institute of China show that the stronger the evaporation of the ground
water is, the bigger the substrate water evaporation is, and the bigger the
accumulation of salt in the soil. Years of research prove that it is best for the ground
water to be controlled at 2 m in spring, 1.5 m in falL I m in sunmmer. This is based on
the characteristics of North China's climate and is a most effective measure to
prevent salinization.
B. Conditions for the Secondary Salinization of the Project Area's Soil
The project site locates on the alluvial plain with a small gradient. Owing
to the Yellow River's alluviation, there is a water-logged terrain with thick earth
layer. The earth comes from the river's alluvial substances in which there are lot of
soluble salts making salinization possible.
The project area belongs to the temperate zone with a half moist monsoon
climate, cold and dry in winter, rainy in summer, quick warming-up and dry in
spring, quick cooling-down and drastic shortage of rainfall in autumn. The
prerequisite of salinization is that the yearly evaporation is bigger than the
precipitation. However, the seasonal interchange of the moist and dry will cause salt
accumulation in spring and salt deduction in summer and salt accumuLkitiot again in
fall.
4-17



The groundwater under the project area is veiy shallow, between 1.0 to 2.5
meters and an easily salinized area. Thiis is one of the main characteristics of the
project area's agricultural ecological environment. If there are no eflective
measures aflcr the project is put in use, it's possible that the ground water level will
rise, causing secondary salinization or water logging.
C. Project's Impact on the Salinization of the Surrounding Area
The project area is subject to the impacts of climate, hydrogeology, hydrobath,
drainage, etc., belongs to the salinization-prone zone and also stands good chance
of getting salinized. The ground water level around the rcservoir remains 2.5 mcters
almost unchangeable, with changes no bigger than one meter. Influenced by Yellow
River's side leakage, the water is difficult to drain. When the pondage reservoir is
put in use, water level of the reservoir is seven meter above ground, dam base
leakage and pressure from the high water level will cause the rise of groundwater
and some areas may even be water-logged, and thus causing the increase in salt
content of the surrounding arable land.
Sedimentation basin is built in the low-lying area. Ground water is 1.0 to 1.5
meter beneath, mineral content 0.7 to 1.2 g/l, soil's salt content 0.076 to 0.90%6.
Besides, the bundings of the sedirnentation basin and the alluvial altitude will cause
an alluvial delta, the length of which will vary in different phase of the operation of
the sedimentation basin. See Table 4. 1. 11.
Table 4.1. 11    Mud's alluvial altitude and elongation of the delta

D. Measures Taken to Mlitigate Impacts
a) Measures Taken to Prevent Reservoir's Leakage
HDPE plastic fim is highly water-proof, adhesive and adaptable and hence the
ideal leakage-proof material. Vertical plastic application has alrcady bccn widely
used in the hvdro-projects. which is convenient in use, cheap in cost and effective
4-1 l



in leakage preventiorL etc. In this project the top laver of sauid soil has a
permeability of 103-10-4 cnm/s. There is a whole layer of soil eight to nine meter
below whose permeability is 104-1 o7 cm/s. So, a single laver of 0.4 millimeter thick,
ten meter wvidens polyethylene film will be applied vertically alongside the
reservoir's bundings. top of the film will meet the film built in the dam, making an
enclosed leakage-proof layer.
b) Leakage Prevention and Leak-age Discharge Mleasures
To discharge the water leaked around the reservoir, some leakage
prevention ditches are needed. The ditches from North Bunding's Dawu Flood
Discharge Sluice to Dawu Water Sluice will be used together with the newly-dug
flood discharge ditch outside the North Stretch Embankment. Leakage prevention
ditches will be dug from Yanjia Vilage. Ditches will be dug outside both the south
and west bundings, the center line of which is 37 meters to the out ring of the water
discharge ditch. The ditches has a bottom width of two meters, a depth of three
meters (the proportion of height to slope is 1:2, while the proportion of bottom
width to slope is 1/10000). The total length of the ditch is 6.95 kilometers in which
north bunding takes up 1.6 kilometers, east 1.3 kilometers, south 3.6 kilometers,
west 0.45 kilometer.
There will be connection ditches every 200 meters between leakage prevention
ditches and water discharge ditches at the foot of the reservoir. The connection
ditches are one meter in bottom width, 1.2 meter in depth (the proportion of height
to slope is 1:1.5, while the proportion of bottom width to slope is 1/5(X0).
There are four tunneLs on the old Jinhu railroad outside the south bunding. By
digging the connection ditches the leakage prevention ditches are connected with
the flood discharge ditches in the North Stretch Zone. The water leaked will be
discharged by the discharging system through Dawu flood discharge sluice and the
flood discharge ditches outside the North Stretch Zone. Besides, check sluice will
be set at the confluence of the leakage prevention ditches to prevent the counter
flow by high water level.
There are seepage prevention ditches in all the directions of the sedimentation
basin except in south. The average height of the seepage prevention ditches is 23
meters above ground, with bottom wNidth of three meters. rhe proportion of height
to slope is 1:2.5, while the proportion of bottom width to slope is 1/5000.
E. The Forecast of the Project's Impact on Soil Secondary Salinization
To mitigate the pro,ject's impact on soil secondarv salinization, at cast, south,
north and west bunding 37 meters away from the dam a leakage prevention ditch
will be built and another at 15 meters away from the east, west and north sides of
sedimentation basin.
The maximum and minimum linear distance between the reservoir and the
sedimentation basin are 2.05 and 1.06 kilometers. respectively. The design of the
reservoir area and scepage prevention ditch around the sedimentation basin are the
same as those of the by-ditch in Yuchencg Yellow River irnigation area. According
4-19



to the research results shown in Report of Comprehensive Management on
Salinization and twenty years' practice, leakage prevention ditch on by-ditch
standards ( depth 3 meters, bottom width 2 meters, the rate of height to slope is 1:2
and the rate of bottom width to slope is 1/1000) can control an area of 5 to 8 square
kilometers. Groundwater has an average drop of 0.23 meter and mineralization of
groundwater has an average drop of 0.305 g/l. Thus it can be controlled between 1
and 2 meter after leakage proof and leakage prevention work is done to the
reservoir and the sedimentation basin. And it can restrain secondary salinization
from occuwning.
4.1.3.2.3 The Forecast of the Project's Sedimentation Basin's Impact
on Land Desertification
A. The lInpact of the Project's Sedimentation Basin and Stockvard's on Land
Desertification
When the project is put into operation, the annual water diversion amount will
be 174,910,000 cubic meter, and the annual sand conveyance of the ditch is 1.191
million cubic meter. The use of the ditch's sedimentation is divided into three stages,
a total of 25 years. The applicable sedimentation area 1.4 square kilometer. In the
sevcnth year, on ditch will be converted into two ditches. The useable water level will
reach its highest of 32.5 meters. Ihe altitude of the dam is 33.5 meters. Tlhe water
inside is 2 meters deep. The mud in the ditch will be dredged and transported to sand
stockyard. The first stage sand stockyard area is about one square kilometer. The
height of the sand pile in first stage is 8.5 meters with time limit of six years, while
the area of second stage is 2 km2 with sand pile height of 6.5 m. So the stockyard is
useable for twelve years. Thus it can be seen, the project's sand conveyance amount
is large, sand sedimentation and pile occupies a wide area and sand pile reaches high.
The use suspension of the ditch's sedimentation basin and fulfill of the sand
stockyard are main factors that cause the desertification.
B. Measures to Mitigate Land Desertification
Main measures taken to prevent desertification are concentrated use of dixided
land. After use, build the dam with mud dredged, plant trees, establish imgation
system and resume cultivadon . Thus desertification can be overcome and
occupation of land can be lessened for developmcnt of agriculture.
C. The Forecast of Desertification
The covering of the sand sediment and resumption of cultivation after use of
the sand stockyard is one of the successful experiences about soil amelioration in the
Yellow River flooding area. And it has been spread to use from the 60's till now.
The irrigation area of Xiezhai in Heze district had been widely using warping ever
4-20



since 1969. The warping area was 6200 hectares. Warping amelior-ates the
cultivation layer of the land. The highly nutritious alluvial lands raises the soil's
nutritious content of the sandy and salty lands after warping and improves its water
and fertility preservation. See Table 4.1.12 and 4.1.13.
Warping raises agricultural production. Dongming county, bordering upon the
Yellow River in the west, has long been drifted and a large sector was formed and
dusty all year around. Before warping, the average output per mu was 115 jin. Since
1976, the project's quality control has been strengthened. Alluviation was introduced
to ameliorate the soil. In 1983, 90.5 thousand jin of grains was contributed to the
countzy. Wangdian Village in the same irigation area has 2,468 mu arable land.
Before warping, the average grain yield per mu was 120 jin with a total of' 296
thousand jin. After warping in 1979, per mu's yield reached 440 jin and totaled 1086
thousand jin, 3.7 times of that before warping.
It follows therefore that, only if overa}l planning is executed in the project area
and input and output is serialized, warping and covering will surely be able to
enhance fertility and physical properties of sand stockyard lands, resume use of the
'land, and attain the goal of making best use of the lands in the sedimentation basin
and sand stockyard and raising the grain yield and refraining from desertification. If
more is invested in agriculture in this area, comprehensive management is executed
and farming done scientifically, ,better results will surely be seen.

4.1.3.2.4 The Analysis orthe Project's Impact on Irrigation System
4-21



and Flood Discharge
A. The Project's Impact on Irrigation System and Flood Discharge
After the complction of the projcct, the sand stockyard and the sedimentation
basin of original inigation area will overlap the east main ditch. The original four
kilometers long main discharge ditch from Nanfan Village to Beizhan and Dawu
flood discharge sluice will be occupied by the reservoir, and this will exert great
itpact on the project area's irrigation system and flood discharge.
B. Mitigation Measures
In the view of making surc the irrigation system and flood discharge system
work properly after the completion of the project, the project is to re-plan and design
the two systems in the area. The original sedimentation basin will be expanded
northwestwards to a new aquaduct, eastwards to Nanfan Village, southward to
Dingkou Village and northward to No.309 highway, and the total area is not changed.
Along the south of the pondage reservoir---the original Jinghu railway and No.309
highway a main outflow ditch will be dug via Dawu flood discharge sluice across the
northem stretch embankment. And then along the northem stretch embankment
eastward the ditch is to be linked with Dashi River, and to be met vith leakage
prevention ditch, and this will basically ensure good uirigation. Besides, at the
confluence of the leakage prevention ditch and flood discharge ditch, a check sluice
will be built to prevent high water level flood water from backflowing into the
leakage prevention ditch.
C. Impact Analysis
After re-planning and dcsigning of the irrigation system in the proicct area,
irigation can be basically ensured.
4.1.3.2.5 Analysis of Impacts of Abstraction from Y'ellow River on Surface
Water in Jinan
A. Current Situation of Water Supply in Jinan
The water supply of Jinan consists of three main water resources-groundzwater,
reservoir water and Yellow River water. The total designed water supply is 880,000
t/d, of which 50,000 t/d from Wohushan &Jinxiuchuan reservoir north of Jinan. in
1983, Jinan Yellow River Water Diversion Works was ratified by the State Planning
committee. The amount of designed water supply is 400,000 t/d. The first project
has already in operation since May, 1989 which provides 200,000 tVd. The second
project is up to be completed, however, it runs in a worse condition because of
shortage of water supply without pondage reservoir.
