5.5.3.8. Conclusion from Assessment
During the period of 1989 to 1994, the coal consumpfion in District Zhifu of Yantai
City increased by 3.8% each year, and the concentration of SO2 in the air also rose by
2.4%, although some pollution controlling measures had been taken in these years. The
monitoring results shows distinct difference of SO2 andrSP concentrations in the
assessment area exists between the district heating period and non- heating period .For
the maximum at any times, Of all the 6 monitoring sites in winter,the concentrations of
the SO exceed the Class 2 of ((National Air Quality Standards)) from time to time
3             0.15M/3
(NAQS Class 2: the maximum at any times 0.50mg/m ,daily average: 0.15 mg/r  )
The radio of exceeding standard limits for SO2 isl2%, and the maximum of SO2 is
0.889 mg/rn exceeding the N A Q S class 3 while in Spring, the maximum at any times
for the SO2 do not go beyond the second standard limits .However, the daily average
concentration of SO2 exceed the second standard limit both in winter and spring, The
radio of the daily average conceniration of SO2 going beyond the second standard limits is
80% in winter,and 60% in spring.The maximum daily average concentration of SO2 is
3 .3
0.375 mg/mi  in wintcr and 0.259 mg/mr  in spring all excced the third standard
limits.The above results shows that the air quality in District Zhifu. of Yantai can not meet
the demands of Class 2 of N A Q S. Some district ( about 20Km2 ) have exceed the
third standard limit.
Taking the Grids of Bearing Factory and the other few representative grids as examples,
The calculation results reveals that the implementation of the proposed projects can cut the
ground level concentration of S02 by more than 62%, and  of TSP by ligher thlan 36%.
This calculation shows that implementation of the proposed project can make the
concentration of SO2 at any times in the Urban area (area: 18 square kn) within the Standard
limit of Class 2, but can not makc it within the Standard limit of Class I (Standard limit: at any
times: 0.1 5mg/m3, daily average: 0.05mg/i3). On a  conservatively cstimate, the guaranteed
ratio of cutting SO2 concentration by 20% is more than 60%, and the air quality can become,
within the Standard limit of Class 2 in all the monitoring sites except the site of Harbour. In
the west suburb of Yantai City, the low cutting ratio of SO2 concentration results from the
fewer replaced boilers by the proposed project, SO2 concentration can be cut by 37.380/o,
and dust by 14.06% in this area. Thne concentrations of the pollutants at any times are
accordingly calculated to still be in the Standard linit of Class 2. If the cutting ratio of SO2 is
20%, the cumulative concentration of SO2 can not become in the Standard limit of Class 2.
The calculation results reveal that the winterly average concentration of SO2 can be cut
by more than 53%, and TSP by more than 20%. Using the Intcmaaional Standard limit of
Class 2 (maximum of yearly average of daily average: 0.06mg/m3, and maximum of daily
avcragc 0.1 5mgrn/3) as references, we propose that the maximum of seasonly average of SO2
544



concentration be 0.lOOmg/m3, then the winterly averages of 502 concentration in all the sites
of urban area can meet the Standard requirements of Class 2 . Therefore, it can be concluded
that implementation of the proposed project can imlprovc the air quality in the urban area of
Yaantai City greatly. The air quality would be ccrtaia to meet the requirements of Class 2 of
the National Standard in aJl the urban area except the special sections like Harbour.

The Standards used in this assessment are (( National Environmental Standards of

A. Model Used for Calculation
Scc Annex 2.
B. Analysis on the Noise Sources
a) On the Sources during Construction Phase
According to the analysis on the proposed project, the noise sources during
construction phase are the construction maclhinery (maximum :1 lOdB(A) from
pneumatic tools) anid tlhc conveyance tools 80 dB(A) to 90 d13(A)..
b) On the Sources during Operation PJhasc
The noise sources of the proposed projcct during operation phase are: water-
recycling pumps andl water-compcnsating pitrips wvhosc noise is in 80 - 90d13(A). In
our calculation, the noise intensity of each pump is treated as 90dB(A), the number of the
pumps in each monitoring site is listed in Table 5.5.4. 1.
C. Results and Analysis
a) In Constluction Phase
In a scope of 50m from the construction site is calculated, the calculated noise from
the pneumatic tools (1 10 dB(A)) is 65dB(A), and that from conveyance tooLs (9OdB(A))
is 45dB(A).
b) In Operation Phase
In a scope of 50m from the noise sources, the calculated noise value in each
monitoring site is less than 35dB(A), witiin the Class 1 limits of Standard (GB3096 -
93).
Among the noise-monitored results of 43 silcs of present noise in the environment
(offered by Yantai Municipal Environmcntal Monitoring Station)' the present maximnum
in daytime is 69.ldB(A), and the minimum is 48.0dB(A); 19 of which exceed the
545



stanidard limits. Thc site whosc prcsent noise exceeds the standard limit most is Site 37,
owing to the effect of building construction; The maximum of monitored noise in night
60.4dB(A), and the minimum is 38.1 dB(A); noise in 14 sites excecds thc standard limit,
and thlc iioisC in sitC 18 xcxeeds the Standard Limits by 10.4 dB(A), the most exceeded
value, due to the traffic effect. The sites whose noise exceeds the; Standard Limits both in
daytime and night arcNo. 1  7. 13 . 14 . 18 , 36 and 39.The noise contribution
in daytime comes from: traffic, daily lile anid construction  only a little from industry.
The noise in night comes mainly fiom traffic. The sites whose noise exceeds the Standard
Limits distributes mainly in central urban arca.
Tlhc accumulativc values of thle calculated and the corresponding monitored sites are
fisted in Table 5.5.4.1. The data marked with * are those exceeding the corresponding

5.5.4.3 Coniclusion
3 The construction machincry such as pncumatic tools can yield high noise to the
environment, so to lesson the effect of nioise from the construction machinery on the
einvironment, the construction time should be arTangged in 8:00-12:00 and 14:00-
18:00 in a day, and the pncumatic tools should be strictly forbidden in night. to
protect the workers from the noise' elect, it's suggested that the workers should be
equipped with protectors.
Our calculation shows that the operation of thc proposed project will has great
effect on the region whose background noise is low, such as the Sites of 28 . 29 and
34i1 Class ! and II Functional Zones, the noise value added is ca; ldB(A). Therefore, the
silencer and sound insulator systems in thc pump stations in these zones should be
improved to minimize the noise effect on the environment.

width is 3 to 5 mi, occupied width by the construction is 6 to 10m. The total dug length is
9,138m. Therefore, the traffic will not be avoided to affect during construction phase;
and the noise, dust arisen from the construction will definitely affect the walking people
and the residents along the construction line.
Construction of the peakload heating boiler house and the hcat consumer stations
needs iorever requisition land with an area of 43,125 mi2, including 525 rn agricultural
field, 30.000m2 land from village-run Brick Factory, and 12,600mm2 urban state-owned
land. Construction of tlec project need no demolishing civil house, it only will remove a
800m2 house owned by the Brick Factory and a 1,650m2 building owned by the Coal
Shop of Municipal Fuel Company. The affected population affected by the
lan(lrcquisilioli and deimolisiing is I] 5.
Thcrc is no minority nationality rcgions in tlc asscssment Irca, no rcscrving zonc of
forestry, no preserving area of culture and ancicnt relic. Although the project area is
coastal arca, the construction the project will have no cffect on the aquatic livings,

5.6 Analysis on the Environment Protection Measures
5.6.1 Environment Protection Measure in the Construction Period
Demonstration Project of Yantai 500 Heating Network Project will have a negative
inpact on cnvironmcnt during its construction phase. Now we try to discuss the way of
alleviate this negative impact.
5.6.1.1  Land was chosen to makc the nctwork involve important production rcsource
as litle as possible.
Nature rcsource protcction area, wet land will not be involved. Wild life biologic
environment and livestock removing line will not be disturbed. Biologic resource such as
forest, grass land will not be destroyed.
Do not destroy any historic products of culture and important culture scenes.
Do not interrupt underground pipelinc and project.
Do not remove resident houses.
Repairing the wrecked road timely.
5.6.1.2 Construction of the networkl will not involve important business streets and main
lines of communication, so as to avoid serious traffic problem. In some parts of roads
where tralfic changed to other rout, the traffic management should be strengthened.
5.6.1.3  According to the  ((Noise Standards for Boundary of Construction Sites))
(GB12523-90), any equipment which do not meet the noise control standard should be
substituted or bc used with mufflers. In case of necessary, the constructors should use
earplug in order to diminish the noise effect on themselves.
5-51



5.6.1.4  The working hours during consiruction pliasc should not be at the resident rest
time. The planned construction time is 8:00-12:00 AM; 14:00-22:00 PM1.
5.6.1.5 The road in construction as well as the sand on iLs sidcs should be watered or
oiled periodically, in order to diminish the dust.
5.6.1.6 Make sign in the construction road section, including red light in night. When
the road wrecked during the pipeline construction, a cross bridge slhould be built for the
pedestrian.
5.6.1.7 The workers doing the projects construction should be chosen under the
following condition:
Choose local worker preferentially to reduce the floating workers( workers from
other part of the countly).
Setup dwelling place for the necessary workers from other part of the countuy.
Setup treatment and collecting facilities for the workers everyday life waste.
Periodically check on the professional health and security, and make necessary
treatment.
5.6.1.8   In spite of the above measures, thlre is unfavorable influence which should
bc diminished during the planning and construction phase.
For the farmland and workshop levied, economic compensation or new settlement
will be arranged.
When the residents' work or everyday life was disturbed in project construction,
appropriate measure should be taken to get the agreement and tnderstanding of the
residents.
Cooperate with local government, subdistrict office to get their support, and make
the construction fields under good management.
By taking above measure, the unfavorable impact of the construction on the
environment can be diminished to the lest.
5.6.2 Environment Protection Measures during Its
Rulning Phase
Demonstration project of Yantai 500 Heating Network Project is an environment
project of replacing the dispersed small bsoicrs and little coal furnace witlh district heating
system. Its purpose is to improve the air quality of the urban central area . Before the
construction of the projct, main pollutants of this area at ordinary monitoring site are:
SO, 0.164 mg/Nm3, TSl': 0.296 mg/Nm3. Aftcr the construction of this project, the
eslimated value at the same site will be SO2: 0.0679 mg/Nm3, TSP: 0.2358 mg/Nm3. It
is obvious that this project will improvc this area's air quality. Because new facilities
-52



slhould l)c setup, such as peak load licating boiler house anid boostcr pump stations, thlrc
will bc unfavorable influence on the cnvironmcnt duIring its running phase. Now we
discuss the unfavorable intluence and its alleviating measure.
5.6.2.1 Air Pollution Control Measures
A. Dcdusting Measures
The bitube water-film dust removcr was used in this projcct. Its dcdusting efficiency
is 98%, the fly ash discharge concentration under the planned construction condition is
84.71 mrg/N\m3, which is in the limits stipulated in the <<Air Pollutants Emrission
Standards for Boilers>>
Investment on the double tube wet-filim dust renmover is about 2,500,000 yuan
(RMMB), higler than that on the ordinary wct-fjhi  dust rcmovcr( lower than that of
electricremover). But its dedusting efficiency is high than ordinary dust remover( close to
that of electric dust remover) It is easy to run and is suitable for peak load boiler house to
run for asuch a short timne.
B. Desulfurizing Mcasures
(1) When the flue gas goes througl the sulfur rcmover in this project, calcareous
water was used as desullurizcr. hlc desullurizing rate was 50%. Under the designed
construction condition, the concentration of S0O in the emission is 539.91 mg/Nm3,and
thc dischargc amount of S02 is 105.84kg/h, within limits sp)ecified in <<Shandong
Provincial Air Pollution Emission Standards>->.
Desulfurizing by calcarcous water is a wet desulfurizing methods. Although it needs
Icss invcstment and is simple to operate, it is casy to form dust, that will block up the pipe
andl cquipment. Thus to guarantee the proper running of this project in a long-tcrm, the
remover must be maintained periodically and correctly.
C. Dust in the Coal Storage Fields
To decrease the coal dust during its load and unload, water spiritiing device with
water cleaner should. be setup.
5.6.2.2 Measures of  Controlling Noise Pollution
According to the regulations of <<Conlrolling Noise in Design of Construction
ProLtccts>> ,wheni choosing device, low noisc equip)men1t shouild considered previously,
high noise dcvice, such as centrifugal pump and blast engine ect. should be used with a
denoiscr and muffler
In order to meet the ´<Noise Standard for the Boundary of Construction Sites>>,
the pumps should be centralized into plant buildings, and be run at a reasonable window
statc (in wintcr time, closc all the windows). Thcre should bc more green field and
enclosure wall around the plant.
Workers in the construction field should use personal protection articles such as
earplug.

For abov/c protccfion measure, it is estinaied that the noisc degree is below
35dB(A) in the ncighborhood, meet the requlrcmcnt of << Noisc Standards for Urban
Area Environment >>. There is no obvious impact on the existing noisc situation, and no
liami lo tlhc workers.
5.6.2.3 Measures for Sludge Treatment
Sludgc of quantity 4367 tun/ycar coming liom the hcat peak boilcr will all be
sent to nearby brickyard for comprehensive usc.
In wet-dcdust system which is used in this project, sludge was temporarily laid in
the sludge pond( within two days). Thus there is no secondary dust pollution.
5.6.2.4 Measures of Water Pollution Controlling
Water pollution controlling is not so important as waste gas in this project.
Because the waste water only comes from daily life which is of small quantity, and not

In a word, during operation phase, thc unfavorable influence can be diminished to

5.7 Altcrnativc Heating Program
The proposed project was first planned in 1987, and formnally put into rccords in
1994. The heating netwvork- was made up under a procedure of through carefully
expounding and proving by related experts, and it also undergoes consultant and
compromise arnong Yantai Municipal Government, Municipal Planning Bureau and
Municipal Heating Power Development Office over and over again. Following is a brief
discussion of this process.
5.7.1 Characteristic of Heating Area
Yantai city is a along the seashorc, and at the foot of mountain, which has a long
distanec betwvcn west and cast and a short distance bctwcn south and north. According
to the requirement of the Municipal Government, all the buildings muLst be constructed in
the arca of its contour line under 70 metcr. Thus all the building in the center area was
concentrated in a narrow region of 3km width  ( south and north direction ) between
coast and mountain. Differences among buildings' ground contour are between 0 to 70
mctcr.
Thcre arc tlirec maii lincs of conmmunication in the ceniter area. Tlbosc arc North
Avenue, South Avenue ( including Zhichu Road) and Baishi Road which are all lay in
wcst an(d cast dircction. Most of the planncd 22 lhcating districts arc on the two sides of
5-54



Soulh Avcnuc starting west from power plant and ending east to  the thlird stect, show
in Fio.5.1.3.
5.7.2  -Icaling Program
5.7.2.1 H1eatiig Mcdia
MIany-year- practice inside anid outside the country thorouglhly proved that the
heating media in the CiHP which is mainly for the purpose of heating should be hot water.
In this project the basic heating source is the hcaling units which is of cxhausting prcssure
0.2047 MPa and temperature 121C. for such a low pressure, and temperature, it is
impossible to reach the farthest user of 8 kilometer directly. Thus from both technical and
economic view, it is reasonable to choose hot water as heating media.
5.7.2.2 I-Icating Linie
Ihe center of Yantai City is an old urban area. The roads are narrow and the
underground pipc lines are concentrated. The main roulc of the heating project is laid out
froni  the west of power plant to the east. For the  users are mostly on the two sides
of the South Avenue, it is optimal to lay the heating line along the South Avenue. But for
the foliowing two considerations, it is also too dillicult to realize. First, the Soutlh Avenue
is across the center area of the city, whiclh divided the city into two parts of North and
South. It is the city's main line of communication. If the project is constructed in the
South Avenue, it will make the already heavy traffic worse and finally paralyzed.
Secondly, thcre are various kinds of municipal pipe line underground of the South
Avenue. There are only 5-8 metcr seclion wherc no pipe line laid.
Thlc othICer bcter choice is along main line of tic Fenghiuang l'ai Road in the
southen City. But sevcral water pipeline for the supply of thc powver plant has been laid
under this road. Therc is no room for the heating netwvork pipe line. Soil under the road is
mostly weatlhering rock, and it will be very difficult for the construction.
For lots of sight survey, investigations, througl compromise and compartment, the
Municipal Government, Municipal Planning Bureau, Municipal Heating Office made out
the proposal of the heating route. There are sonic  advantages in this proposal. For
example, thc foremost section of 5Km heating nctwork- is built on stilts, which has no
impact on the traffic, do not destroy the road. and do not occupy the site of underground
pipe line. The rcar section of 3Km are not at the main line of communication which has
relativehl little influence on the traffic. But there are also some disadvantages in this
proposal,
The main line divcrlcd the concentrated hcat load arca, which increases the length
of the branch line of the heating network, and then increases the heat loss. Construction
in the mountainous region bring some difficulties for the convey of vehicles and
maclhitncs.
*                            ~~~~~~~~~~~~~5-55



During tle fielk visit, we noticed lhat thic pipc linc located above the Ruwi
Mountain is only 1 meter high to the suiface of the Mountain. For this area's high
elevation and that there is only a distance of about 10 mcters to the northcast border of
thc waste trcatment plant, if the waste treatnment plant extend to the northcast direction,
there surely will be some influence on the pipe line. We investigated this situation and
learned from related local department that the waste treatment plant take an area of 77400
square meter, the waste filled is 1,800,000 ton, there is no room for the development to
the northwest directiop, the planned developmcnt is on the direction of southeast, the
plant will not develop in the direction of the pipe line and there will be no influence on the
pipe line.
We also noticed that there are several cow grazed near the waste treatment plant.
Considering the secondary pollution of the treatment plant and iLs bad effects on the
hcalth of cow, Wc suggcslcd that rclaled department give altctlion to this mattcr, anid
tak-c a measure to restrict the grazing region around the waste treatment plant.
It can be seen from the above discussion, of the threc proposals, each one has
some advantages and disadvantages. But fromn a whole view, under the condition of
settling the waste filling direction problem, the third proposal are practical. Considering
the cnvironmental benefits, the third proposal has least impact on the environment.
5.7.2.3 Peak Load Boiler House
According to the data of the power plant, thcre are two heat sources whose volume
of 460 t/h, an exhausted temperature of 121 ∞C, and an pressure of 0.2047 Mpa. Due to
the conformation of stcam turbine unit (from pure condensed unit to heat supply unit)
and limited electricity load, such an exhausting volume can just meet the demand of a
basic heating, cannot be used as a peak heating source. Generally, in the project of
combination of heat-power, it is also economically unfeasible for the basic heat source
of tlhc power plant to meet all heat load. Thus a peak load heating source must be selup
outside the power plant.
Regional boiler house supplying the peak load heat is the main way in the
combination of heat-power. By this way, the power plaiit can run continuously and
efficiently. It can make the best of the energy-saving of this combination of heat-power.
As mentioned above, the peak load boiler house will be made up by two kinds of
boilcr house. one is the temperature increasinig boiler house, and the other is the end-pipe
boiler house (that is boiler house which remain some original region). The temperature
raising boiler house is serial to the first heater of thle power plant, which functioned as the
peak load heater of the plant. Comparing to the combined heat supply by the regional
boiler house, there are following advantages:
Big boiler ( 4 boilers of 29MW each, while regional boiler lhas only less than 10
MW) has high heat efficiency and  good for energy-saving. It also has complete
dedustfig and desulphurizing devices and can lighten the environment pollution.
S-56



There is no heating network circulatory system of its own. It is unnecessary to set
up circulating wvater pump and relatcd water treatmcnt facilitics. This can simplify the
boiler houLse cuipmcnt, save the slarling invcstmcnt and have a lowcr running cost.
In the running period, the recycling water volume of the first grade network can
be adjusted to avoid the fluctuation of water power due to the operation interruption in
rcgional boiler houses. When the appropriate numwber of scts was choosing, the heater can
start to run set by set to mect the system's requiremcnt of parametcr adjusting, and to
maintain the boiler nning at a high efficiency.
From above analysis, the proposed project of using power plant of Huang-Bo-Hai
Heat and Power Company as basic heating source, the temperature raising peak load
boiler house and some of the existed regional boiler house as peak load heat source is
reasonable and feasible from both the view of economy and environment.

Measures of No. 3 CHP Plant in Weihai

6.1 Pro jcet Analysis
6. 1.1 Location
Wcihai No. 3 CI-IP Plant is located in Southem Urban Area of Weihai city, 0.5 kim

area of tlhc city. See Fig. 6.1.1.
6.1.2 Brief Introduction of the Project
Wcihai No.3 Tlhcermal IPower Plant is a newly-built plant. It will be equipped with
3 sets of 75t/h forced circulation fluidizcd bed boilcrs, mating with 2 sets of CC12-
4.9/0.98/O.294 turbine. Telc project includes the construction of tlhcrnal power plant,
stcam pipe network, f;st grade hot water pipe network and heating thermodynamic
stations. The steam pipe network would be 17.2 knm, which provides steam for the
produclion of 24 entell)riscs and central air condilioning of 12 buildin&gs of 22.6. 1U4
m2 . Thne hot water pipe network would be 12.9 km., whichi proiddes heating for the
buildings of 109.8x1104 mn in this district.
The total investiment of this project amounts to 300.2 million ICK13, including an
expended loan of 144.9 million RMB from the World Bank, converting into 17.25
million US dollars. The plant covers an area of 12x 104 m2 with 375 employees.
6.1.3 Industrial Process
Alter bcing IIixed witli desulphuiizCs (limestotC) and crushed, the coal wil be
sent to the boilers thlrough transferring system. In boilers the chemical energy of coal is
transformed into heat energy to produce steam to drive turbo-generators, changing
mcclianlical cnergy into electrical energy, clectricity is seint to users througlh
transmission and distribution systcm. Meanwhilc, part of the steam, aftcr its doing
workl in the turbines, is extracted to the users for industrial and heating purposes. The
remained steam from turbines is discharged into a vacuum condenser to make
condenscd water, which together wvith boiler replenishing water is heated by steps
tlhrougl regeneration system and then pumped back into boilers, becoming steam
agaitn, tlius foniung a hcat-electiicity combined produclion system with recycling
steam atnd water.
The sulfur removal efficiency in the circulation fluidized bed boiler can reach
X55.,. Thc flue gas is dedusted by electrostatic precipitator then exit in lo thc air

C. 1Ilic Impacts of Sca anid Lind Winid Cirictilationi lo Atmospheric Pollution
The impacts of sea and land wind circulation to atmospheric pollution are generally
caused bv circulatory function and go--and-back function, which means the sea wind
brings baick the pollutant that has been carried to the sca to the tliermal power plant and
seashore area during the sca and land wind transformation period.  By analyzing the
data of actual mcasurement, the included angle of upper and lower layer circulation is

The reserve depot of Weihai No.3 Thermal Power Plant locates in a small gully on
north slope of Baohu I-Ell, 1.5 km southwest of plant site. INs lotal occupied area is
42000m2 with a storing capacity of 150 thousand tons, which satisfy the requirements of
storing adjustment when the way of comprehensive utilization is blocked. The depot is
mainly farmland at present.
Thirough the analysis of the hydrogeological conditions of the reserve cinder depot,
the thickness of weathered elurium in the depot is less than 3 meters, which belongs to
the penneable stratum. Base rock is granite paragneiss which has bad watery and water
permeability. The depot groundwater has no close connection with the groundwater of
neighboring hydrogeological units, but locates at the upper reaches of groundwater
collection area of Xiqufu in northeast.
The belt-like cinder depot is set up along the slope gully, with a high supcrelevation
in longitudinal direction (the average falling gradient is 8%). The cinder should be
stored in steps from the top. When starl using the upper gDid, a dam must be constructed
in the lower grid, where the ash water would precipitale. Once a glid is fill-stored, cover
it witl sofl and plant turf. The rain coud rm off on the suiface without much
permcation. If the eluvial water only exists in the storing grid, its inpacts on surface and
ground water can be controlled. li fact, the main impact factors of eluvial water are PH,
total hardness, F and As. So long as taking proper measures, the forning of eluvial
wvater can be prevented. In wet season, the cinder has a short acting limc on the water.
The pollutants in the cluvial water has a comparatively low density.  After the soil
absorption and puriification, it would not bring functional damage to the water quality of
groundwater catchlnent area in its lower reaches. So, the cinder site selected is
practicable if taking necessaiy controlling measures in using time.

6.5.2.5 Prevention and Control Measures of Noise Pollution
Considering the characteristics of equipment that installed in Weihai NQ 3 CIIP
Plant and its noise features. We put forward the following suggestions:
*  Pay great attention to the noise sources. At the equipment ordering time, require the
manufacturer supply equipment with the noise value not higher than design standard.
To some special equipment with higher noise level, such as coal crusher,
turbogenerator set, blower. Their installation needs to put anti-vibrator, dig anti-
vibration ditch, cover the turbogenerator with blimp, put celotex board around coal
crusher, cover the air compressor with blimp and install it in isolated room. Cooling
tower is also put up isolatedly. Put silencer on the air inlet and outlet of blower,
turbine and air compressor.
* Take sound insulation measures on the windows and doors of plant buildings which
should be airfight.
* In the architectural design, the main work and rest places should be away from noise
sources. And some necessary maintenance rooms should be put up to isolate the
worker from noise.
*  In the general plan of plant area, stress on proper arrangements and noise proof
spacing. Set up afforested belt in plant area, and inside, outside of plant boundary to
reduce the impacts of noise on the surrounding environment.
6.6 Impact Analysis of Ash and Cinder and Coal
Dust on Environment
6.6.1 Ash and Cinder Removing System
626



The ash removed hydraulically and the cinder manually in Weihai CHP Plant
amount to 70,800 tla every year and are dclivered to cement plant, construction
material plant and units for capital construction, paving roads and agricultural
construction to be used comprehensively. These units and plmnts have becn identified.
There is a transfer depot within the plant and an urgent depot in a gully 1.5 km
southwest of the plant to store the ash and cinder delayed in the process to be used
comprehensively.
6.6.2 Treatment of the Ash and Cinder
The pollution degree of the dust is related to the amount of water in the ash and
the weather conditions. That the ash is kept wet in a certain degree will keep the dust
and ash from floating everywhere. The following measures are taken to prevent the
second pollution of the floating dust:
*  Certain amount of water is shed regularly on the cinder-transfer spot to keep it
wet;
*  The urgent cinder storage depot is di%ided into several parts;
i  An afforested belt is built outside the walls of the urgent cinder storage depot to
decrease the amount of the floating dust and to improve the environment;
*  When one part is filled with dust, it is covered with earth to mak-e arable fields and
grass and trees are planted there;
*  The power plant will assign experts to manage the cinder spot and condtuct
regular measurement of the atmosphere around every cinder spot so that
problms will be timely spotted and fimely resohled.
6.6.3 Impact of Coal Dust on Environment and the
Treatment Measures
Ineffective treatment measures and the coal dust pollution in the coal storage
depot are problems polluted in power plant, so prevention and control measures must
be taken in the design. The following measures will be taken with emphasis at this
phrase:
*  Large number of trees will be planted around the cinder depot to forn a
protective belt to decrease the impact of the dust upon the atmosphere.
* Sprinkling system will be installed at the coal depot to shield water regularly and
there will be a sprinkler head every 25 meters so that the whole pile of the coal
can be covered. 21/m3 of water will be shed every time to keep certain humidity
(water>7%) and decrease the amount of the floating dust.
* Hydraulic clearing facilities are installed at the coal delivering bridge, all the
transferring stations and on the tube shaped silo to remove coal dust and prevent
the second pollution of coal dust. The investment in environmental protection will
result in good environmental and social efficicncy, enabling the discharged
pollution of the power plant meet the requirement, decreasing the negative impact
of the discharged pollution upon the environment and improving environmental
6-27



conditions. Power plant project is an environmental protection project and it is
better to build a power plant in terms of improving the living quality of the people.
*  Big duster or electrostatic duster is installed at the transferring station with great
drop height or at the place where coal breaker is set.
*  Drainage and coal depositing reservoir are dug around the coal storage depot to
collect the coal water that is shed or comes from the hydraulic cleaning system
and recollect the mud coal in the coal depositing reservoir.
*  After the coal depot is put into use the power plant will conduct strict
management over it and the sprinklin  hydraulic cleaning and dust removing
facilities will be put into operation in compliance with the demand of the design.
6.7 Environmental Impacts Analysis in Construction
Period
The construction of the project includes plant site and pipe network construction.
The poluting impacts come from the blowing dust and noise of operating equipment.
6.7.1 Impacts of Blowing Dust on Environment and the
Treatment and Control Measures
6.7.1.1 lmpacts Analysis orBlowing Dust on Environment in the Plant
Construction Period
The blowing dust mainly comes from the earthwork phase (the beginning period).
Blowing dust sources are excavator, bulldozer, loading conveyer and other
transportation equipment. The blowing dust includes the dust from earth drop of
excavator, dust caused by catcrpillers and tyres, transportation dust and wind blowing
dust. Because of the short period of earthwork phase (1-2 month) and 1-2 meters high
walLs around the construction site. And the blowing dust has a lower height in operating
time, and a near landing distance, its impacts on the villagers of Songiiawa (0.5 km south
of plant site ) and Zhonglicun (1 km south of plant site ) are quite less.
6.7.1.2 Impacts Analysis of Blowing Dust on Environnment in Pipe
Network Construction Period
The pipe of this project is mostly installed underground. Ihe pipe netvork
construction period includes digging phase, installment phase and covering phase. The
blowing dust in construction period comes from the digging phase, the mound, the
excavator and spade used in digging the pipe ditch. The width and depth of the ditch is
usuallv within 1-2 meters. Lower drop of earth makes little dust, and the landing distance
is also quite near. The dust would not influence the life of the residents in the less
populated south district. After the installment of pipe netwvork;, it must be tesled for
airtight performance. In this period, the mound would be piled along the road for a long
6-28



time. The blowing dust caused by wind probably influence the residenis life. Some
measures should be taken to reduce the dust.
6.7.1.3 Dust Controlling Measures
During the construction period, build up walls of 1 or 2 meters high arounid the
plant site in order to reduce the scattering of flowing dust; Improve the digging speed;
Avoid working in strong wind weather; Lower the drop of earth in operating process;
Take the digged earth to fill pits and make fields. In transportation process, cover the
truck with dust proof sheet. Spray water regularly on the mound along the road. If
these measures are carnied on, the influence of dust to environment would be reduced to
minimum.
6.7.2 Environmental Impacts Analysis of Noise in
Construction Period and thle T'reatment and Control
Measures
6.7.2.1 Impacts Analysis and Assessment of Construction Noise on

structure phase and trim phase.

Main noise sources in earthwork phasc are excavator, bulldozer, loadino conveyer,
tip truck and other transportation vehicles. The sound level of the main sources are from
80 to 90 dB(A).
Through the projection. the range of noise impacts on Songijiawa in this phase is
55.4-66.4 dB(A). The range of impacts on Zhonglicin is 50.3-60.3 d13(A). Noise

7 Environmental Benefits and Losses of
Shandong Environmental Projects
Shandong Environmental Projects includes four projects: Yantai 500 Hlcaating
Network, Weihai No.3 CHP Plant, Jinan Yellow River Water Supply Pondage Reservoir
and Jinan Waste Water Networl. AfRer the implement of these four projects, it will
greatly improve the local environmental quality, push the development and open-up of
the cities forward, bzing about positive impacts on local social and economic
development
Following are the analysis of these projects from the point of Oiew of economic,
social and envirornental benefits.
7.1 Jinan Yellow River Water Suppluy Pondage Reservoir
Project
7.1.1 Economic Benefits
The investment of the project is 499.46 million yuan, including 23 million dollars
(197.80 million yuan) from World Bank, 100 million yuan from Banks in China, 50
million yuan from Shandong Government, 151.66 million yuan from Water Supply
Fund. The water supply volume afler normal operation is 154.51 million cubic meter per
year. So the annual income of the project is 115.88 million vuan. The benefits in the first
year afler operation will be up to 7.767 million yuan.
The eamning ratio of total investment is 12.12∞O, which is larger than the reference
ratio of the line. The payoff period is 8.78 years.
From the analysis above, the earning of this project is relatively high.
7.1.2 Social and Environmental Benefits
Jinan is a historic city famous for its springs. But in the past few years with the
development of the economic reform and construction, water has fallen into shorter
supply. Groundwater resources have been overused. Reservoirs' guarantee rate is only
85%o. Although the Yellow river water resources was put in use in 1988, its watcr supp4y
was always in a low efficiency due to the lack of a pondage reservoir, especially in the
past two years when the Yellow River's drv-up period elongated ( The drv-up period in
1995 was 85 days). That caused the obsolescence of the No. 2 Yellow River Water Plant
(water purification plant ) which already has water supply capacitv of 400.000 tons per
day. It is estimated that in 2000 the highest daily water demand wvilI hit 1.3 million tons
and there will be 300.000 tons short every day.
In this urgent situation, if there are not any pondage reservoiis or new water
resources put in use in 1997, 20-309o of the whole city will be in short in water supply
during the Yellow River's dry-up period. By that time, water supplv will he a chief
7-1



factor hindering the city's social and economirc development. Not only wvoi't thelre be
any chance to restore or retain the natural scenery characteristic of the springs. but also
the economic development and improvement of pcople's living standaird vill lbe greatly
hampered. The implement of this proiect will mitigate the crisis of water supply in Jinan
and satisfy the need of water supphl arouid ycar 2000. which will be helpful to
coordinated development of social economics and environnent. In onc halnd. it will
satisfv the demand of domestic and industrial use. In the other hand. it wilU reduce the
extraction of groundwater, make the water level of grounidwater rise anid tlowinig of
springs, which will also lay the foundation of developing the tourist industries.
7.2 Jinan Waste Water Nethorik Project
7.2.1 Economic Benefits
The investment of the project is 256.95 million yuan, if the inflation is taken into
consideration as required by World Bank, the investment wil be 282.65 million uan.
The earning ratio of total investment is 22.34%o. The payoff period is 1 1.29 years.
From the analysis above, the eaniing of this project is rclative-l high andi the risk is
low.
Jinan Wa*stewater Treatment Plant had becn finished the lirst stage enginleering wilt
the investment of 0.305 billion Xuan (capacity: 0.22 million m3 d). But, it can not be put
into use due to lack of pipeline network. The annual salar cost of the plant will hit 9.6
million yuan (160 persons, average salarm: 500 vuanrmonth per cipita). If the discount
rate of fixed assets is 4.5%, the discount fee is 13.7 million yuan per year. so the annual
loss of the treatment plant will hit 20 million yuan added by interests of loans. After the
implement of the project, this kind of losses can he avoided.
7.2.2 Environmental Benefits
At present, most of industrial and domestic wastewatcr are discharged without aniv
treatment process and bring about severe pollution to Xiaotling Riiver and tle rivcr
channels in urban area. Daming Lake already shows the eutrophic charactelistics
polluted by domestic sewage. After the completion of' the network, the operation of

7.2.3 Social Benefits

data, the morbidity of cancer, exogenous febrile disease, hepatitis, enteropathy and skin

Network as parts of the infrastructure will bring about inuneasurable indirect benefits. In
a word, the project is feasible.

7.3.3 Social Benefits



With the completion and running of this project, the municipal infrastructure of
Yantai City will be perfected, its service function will be strengthened and its investment
climate will be improved. This will motivate the city's development and its open
economy.
With the executive of the project, the local atmospheric qualitv is improvedl. Thus
the health leveL the living standard and the sanitation state of the target people are
improved. The residents are relieved from the heavy homework. They have more easy
time to get more rest and entertainment. They can concentrate their efforts to work and
study and to make more wealth for the society.
Because large and small coal supply plants in the city area will be removed, it will
not only save the city land, but also relieve the work-ers in the those plants from heavy
and dirty labor of loading-unloading coals and honeycomb briquette producing. Most of
them become the workem of heat exchange stations. Their labor strength is lightened,
and their income increased.
For the district heating of this projcct, coal can be decreased bv 210,0M) ton each
year (1555 ton each day); sludge transported can be decreased by 65,000 ton each year
(467 ton each day), vehicles used for the transportation decreased by 505 each year.
There are some effects on lightening the city's heavy traffic, diminish the noise and the
prevent the second time dust pollution.
7.4 Wcihai No. 3 CHP Plant
7.4.1 Economic Benefits
The total investment of this project is up to 300.2 million yuan, including 144.9
million yuan (17.25 million US dollar) from World Bank. Its annual is 2 ' 12MWA7. All the
economic indexes of this project can meet the relative national standards. The pay back
period is 8.77 years, which is shorter than the standard (10 vears). The eamino ralio of
total investment is 20.03∞,o (15 years) and 21.36∞%, (20 years), larger thani basic caninig
ratio (120%). Afler operation, the annual income of the plant will hit 144.99 million yuan.
So the economic benefits of the project is high.
7.4.2 Environmental and Social Benefits
Weihai is a newly built coastal city. Along with the development ol the city aild
raise of living standard, the boilers for heating increase greatly. Due to the small capacity,
low heat efficiency, none or low efficiency of dust removal, no desulfirization facilities,
low emission heights it will bring about hcavy pollution.
To improve the ambient air quality in Weihai, the No. 3 CHP Plant is urgently
needed. The operation of the project will not onlv bring about economic bencfits.
increase employment opportunities, but also improve air quualitv and raise thi living
standards of the people. By comparing the circumstances with and without the project,
we know that the construction of No. 3 CHP Plant will further improving the ambient air
quality in Shinan District of Weihai. Shinan District is the industrial zone in Weihai, in
7_c



the following years, all the newly built projects will be constructed in this area, so the
CHP Plant is necessary.

some unfavorable impacts on environment, so the environmental investment is necessary.
The environmental investments will bring about good environmental and social benefits
and'greatly reduce the unfavorable inpacts caused by construction of the projects.

A. Reservoir's Seepage Control Measures
There is a compound soil film on the box dam of the reservoir and a seepage
control soil film vertically under the ground. There is a seepage prevention film formed
by connecting the dam slope with the dam foundation.
B. The Seepage Prevention Measures in Box Dam of Reservoir and Sedimentation
There is a escape canal close to the dam foundation in the lower reaches of the box
dam, which is used to collect the vadose water, which will be discharged into seepage
control ditch. The distance between its center and outside adge of.discharging ditch is 37
m. The width and depth of escape canal are 2 and 3 m repectively. The proportion of its
height to its slope is 1:2, while that of width to slope is 1/10000.There is a transverse
escape canal cvcry 200 meters between the escape canal and seepage control ditch, with
the wvidth of onc mcetr and dcpth of two mcetrs. 'I'hc proportion of its hcight to its slope
is 1:1.5, while that of width to slope is 1/5000. By means of using the escape canal, the
water level in the ditch should be kept two meters below the ground. The transverse
escape canal which connected the seepage control ditch with flood discharge gully in the
stretch zone wvill discharge the vadose water to Dawu flood discharge gate, finally to Dasi
River. Three directions except in south of the sedimentation also has the seepage control
ditch, ftllcen meters away from the dam willt Ihc widdt of thrce meters. The average
height of the foundation is twenty three meters. The proportion of its height to its slope is
1:2.5, while that of width to slopc is 1/5000.
C. Rational Planning of Irrigation and Drainage System of Farmlands in Project Area
The irrigation system should be redesigned. The former sand basin of irrigation
IIIovCs nortlivest nearby the new delivery pipcline.
To assure the discharge of vadose water, a new escape canal will be constructed
along the Dawu flood discharge gate northward to stretch zone and finally, all the vadose
watcr vill be dischargcd into Dasi River.
After all the measures taken, the secondary salinization caused by water level rise of
groundwater around the reservoir and sedimentation basin will be alleviated.
D. Strengthen Agricultural and Biological Measures
The using of organiic fertilizer and strawvs will increase the fertility of soil as well as
prevcntion of salinization. As confirmed by China's Agricultural Scientific Institutc, if
the contents of organic matter in the soil is up to 1.5%, it will control the sanlinization.
The higher the content of organic matters, the stronger the function of controlling the
sanlinizationi. If the leveling of farmlands, intensive and mcticulous farming and scientific
cultivation can be combined, the effects will be better.
E. Second Ploughing Timcly, Preventing the Desertification after Stop Use of
Sedimentation and Sand Heap Basin
The second ploughing after stop use of sedimentation and sand heap basin is a
successful experience. It will reduce the occupation of the land as well as prevent the
desertification trend.

F. Flood Protection Measures
The relative flood protection measures must be executed according to the
regulations of Yellow Rivcr Committee of Ministry of Water Conservancy.
G. Prevention Measures for Water Pollution and Eutrophication in the Reservoir
1. Build good comprehensive planning. The control objective of nitrogen and
phosphorus are 0.6 and 0.04 mg/I, respectively. Irnplement total discharge amount
control. The main task of Queshan Reservoir is to assure the water supply to
industrial and domestic use. Hence, the building of comprehensive treatment
planning is very important. Implement total discharge amount control to main
pollutants. Assure the nutrition level of the reservoir keeping in the state of middle-
cutrophication.
2. Practical measures should be taken to control the over input of nitrogen and
phosphorus.
a) Increase the height of inner of the reservoir to prevent surface run-off from
entering into the reservoir. All diversion holes in the buildings in project area should
lower than water level of the reservoir to prevent the cntry of pollutants.
b) Before the operation of the reservoir, the measures such as washing and
discharging all the water after fifteen days of pondage should be taken to reduce the
content of nitrogen and phosphorus.
c) According to the design, after operation of the reservoir, it is estimated that there
is still 89,000 tons sand entering the reservoir cvciy year. The sand has the function
of absorption of nitrogen and phosphorus. So cleaning the deposits regularly will
reduce the deposit of pollutants and prevent the reservoir from marsh swamp.
d) All the watcr delivery pipeline are laid underground.
c) To assurc the water quality, if thc water level of the reservoir is lower than twenty
four meters, the water will not be used.
f) In the outer of the reservoir, Bushes and gra.sses should be planted.
3. Remove the planktonic alga. When in high temperature season, the removing
measures should be taken to prevent breeding of the alga.
4. The abstraction should avoid the period just after Yellow River's dry-up.
5. The environmental management institutions should assure the monitoring of water
quality proceeding in nonnal and effective way. Nitrogen and pho.sphorus should be
strictly controlled.

10.2 Assessment Conclusions and Suggestions of Yantai
500 Heating Network
10.2.1 Conclusions
10.2.1. 1 Conclusions from the Project Analysis
In thiis project, the surplus heat of the Huang-Bo-H-ai Heat-Power Company is used
as basic heat source, three existed boiler houses and one peakload heating boiler house to
be built are used as peak load heat sources to meet the demand of peak load heat-
supply. This proposal is made out on the basis of thoroughly proving, compromising and
balancing among the Municipal Govermnent, Municipal Planning Bureau, Municipal
Heat-Power Development Office and related specialists.
D Encrgy Utilization
Now, in Huang-Bo-Hai Heat-Power Company, there are two generating sets of
power 100MW, which is used only to generating electricity, its energy efficiency is about
40%. After the completion of this project, the energy utilization ratio will be over 80%,
increased by more than one time.
* Heating Media
Thc heating media is hot water. Lots ol practices inside and outside the counity
show that the district heating system is reasonable from both the technical and economic
xiews, but in the cases steam draw pressure of the basic heat source is 2047MPa, the
temperature of thc hcating engine is 121'C, the heat can not be sent to consumors in a
distance of 8 km. Thus, in this project, the optimal choicc of th heat media is hot water.
* Supplementary Heat Sources
Considering the reformation of the steam reception engine, and the economical
reasonability, a peak load heating boiler house will be setup outside the ILuang-Bo-ILai
Heat and Power Company. In this prcject, there are two kinds of the peak load boiler
house, onc is the pcak- load heating boiler house, the other is the three existed regional
boiler houses. Compared with the proposal of combined basic heat source and the
regional boiler house, this project has following advantages: high eti ciency, fuel saving,
high dedusting and desulfuning ef iciency, low cost of operation, and stable operation
due to the adjustable water-amount in the primary circuit.
* Network Establishment
In this project, total heat pipe line is 30 Km long. Two thirds of them directly
buried underground. In this way, the heat pipe line are mainly laid on the well built road
in order to cut down the length of the pipeline, be convenient to the connection of the
sccondary circuit, avert the removing of the resident lhouses. But duting the construction
phase, traffic will be influenced due to the road wrecked. So in the designing of the
project, Ihe principles are: the least possible pipe line will be used, the least road be
1U-9



wrcckcd, anid main road of business and main lines of conmunication should be averted
in order that no traffic block be caused. Thus lhcrc will be no senrous traffic problem in
the construction phase of the pipeline network.
Pipeline built on stilts is about 5 Km long distributed in the suburb. The pipeline
will be built over such a height that vehicles, people livestock can communicate freely.
*  The Newly Added Pollution Sources.
i) Air
In this project, the newly added air pollution source is the 80 meter high chimney of
the peak load heating boiler house, whose coal consumption is 22,180 t/y, SO2 emitted
is 111.79 ton, ily ash cmittcd is 17.54 ton cachi year. Tshe cniissions are within the limits
Class 1 of <<Air Pollution Emission Standards for Boilers> (GB13271-91) and <<
Shandong Provincial Waste Gas Pollutant Emission Standards>> (DB371006-91).
ii) Waste Water
The waste water in this project comes mainly from the newly added heating boiler
house, slag-scouring water and daily life waste water.
The largest amount of waste water from the boiler house is 15 ton per day, which is
not discharged, but led to the dust-precipitation tank and used as slag-scouring
supplementary water.
The largest amount of the dust-wash-out sludge is 40 ton per hour, which is not
discharged, but is circulated after filtering and sediment.
The largest amount of daily life waste water is 36 ton each day, 2000 ton each year,
whlich is dischatged to the urbane sewage network system, and be in the centrally
treated plant of the city.
iii) Waste Residue
The waste residue is only produced from the tiewly added boilcr by 4.13 ton per
hour, which is transported to the Yantai Light Building MateriaLs Factory for
comprehensive use.
iv) Noise
a. During Construction Phase
The main source of noise is construction machine, which meet the requirement
of ´thc Noisc Standard Limit in the  Boundary of Construction Sites>>. (GB12523-
90). To make less disturbance to the residents, the construction time is arranged in the
day tinme.
b. During Operation Phase
The main source of noise is the blast engine, air draw engine of the new added
boiler and the newly built 42 heat consumers heat stations, which meet the requirement
of the c Regulations for Controlling Noise in Industrial Enterprise Designing >>
(GBJ87-85).

10.2.2 Suggestions
10.2.2.1 Dedusting and Desulfurizing Efficiency of Large Boiler are
to be Improved
From the pollution source investigation, we know that 290 industrial boilers, 63,000
civil-used stoves and cooking boilers will be rcplaced by the project. Thc boiler's
replacemcnt ratio is 64.73%. The cuL ratios of SO2 and fly ash are 19.89% and
34.03% respectively. This reductioh ratio is not so high due to the low cut ratio coal-
consumption ( total cut ratio of coal is 14.21%). Alter implementation ol the project, the
total coal-consumption by industrial boilers is still 1,233,200 ton per year. S02 and fly
ash discharged are respectively 26,998 ton and 6802 ton each year. In this investigation,
we noticed that most of industrial boilers had been provided with circulated blast
dedusting devices, its efficiency is about 80%, but there are no desulfurizing measures. It
is estimated that if the dedusting and desulfurizing efficiency increased by 20% and 15%
respectively in the boilers not to bc replaced, the emissions of SO and fly ash will
respectively be decrcase by 5,400 ton and 1,020 ton each year, equal to the amount of
S02 and TSP cut by this proposed project. ( In the project, SO, and fly ash of boilers
can be decreased by 4428 ton and 1050 ton each year respectively). The environmental
bencfits is sizable. The well operated watcr-flLm dedusting device with 0.8% lime
granulate for desulfurizing has this efficiency. We suggest that related Govenmmental
Departments pay attention to taking the desulfrizing measures in large industrial boilers.
In case necessary, the government should make clear regulations on desulfurizing, and
enforce the laws powerffilly.
